#### 2.2.1.1.0-2 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs Pre-Scheduler overview (ID: 11147570)

**2.2.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147577`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs The pre-scheduler maintains the “pre-scheduler candidate set” (5G_L2_226) of UEs with resource requests of downlink direction (such as VoIP or data transmission, or HARQ retransmission). This set contains a list of UEs that are categorized in resource request classes defined in 5G_UP_ALG_9465_replaced([11174010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuXqrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) excluding ‘systemInformation’ and ‘paging’, each UE belongs to only one resource request class and the highest priority class among all it’s serving cells (in case of CA) is selected.

[CB012734-E] If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, the DL pre-scheduler maintains in addition a list per beam for the DL DRB traffic request class. The UE with this request class is added to the list associated with its primary beam. [End CB012734-E]

In each list, new UEs are added to the back of the list, such that UEs are ordered by the age in the list (5G_L2_226). The UEs in this set meet the criteria defined in 5G_UP_ALG_4185_replaced([11174341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Pre-scheduler Candidates Based on Buffer Utilization”, 5G_UP_ALG_18928_replaced([11174508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (pending RACH Msg2 / Msg4 and SRB0) and 5G_UP_ALG_22397_replaced([11174529](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (pending retransmission), with exceptions defined in any of following requirements:

[Before CNI-127108]

- 5G_UP_ALG_4188_replaced([11174351](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (user setup reception for SgNB addition)

- 5G_UP_ALG_4189_replaced([11174355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Measurement Gap (MG) handling for SA”

- 5G_UP_ALG_22395_replaced([11174363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (beam failure recovery)

[CNI-127108]

- 5G_UP_ALG_4188_replaced([11174351](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "user setup reception for SgNB addition"

- 5G_UP_ALG_4189_replaced([11174355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Measurement Gap (MG) handling for SA"

- 5G_UP_ALG_22395_replaced([11174363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "beam failure recovery"

[End CNI-127108]

- 5G_UP_ALG_8181_replaced([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Reception of PsUser_UserModifyReq” (force DCI 1-0 transient phase)

- 5G_UP_ALG_4196_replaced([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Excluding UE from Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set” (PUCCH F3 transient phase, HARQ A/N feedback confliction with SR/CSI report)

- 5G_UP_ALG_6609_replaced([11174409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Excluding UE from Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to SCell release”

- 5G_UP_ALG_4201_replaced([11174422](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8E_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to A-CSI scheduling with large k2 timing and no k1 available”

[CNI-127108]

- 5G_UP_ALG_14878_replaced([11174430](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL pre-scheduler candidate set due to HARQ-AN bit size restriction"

- 5G_UP_ALG_23479_replaced([11174440](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8F_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL pre-scheduler candidate set due to BetaOffsets update"

- 5G_UP_ALG_25360_replaced([11174462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set on Scell due to reconfiguration"

- 5G_UP_ALG_25378_replaced([11174474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set on Scell due to Measurement Gaps"

[End CNI-127108]

- 5G_UP_ALG_4204_replaced([11174481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Check UE DRX status”

[Before CNI-127108]

- 5G_UP_ALG_4205_replaced([11174491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (URLLC)

- 5G_UP_ALG_4208_replaced([11174539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (User Stop/Delete and SCell release).

[CNI-127108]

- 5G_UP_ALG_4205_replaced([11174491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "URLLC"

- 5G_UP_ALG_4208_replaced([11174539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "User Stop/Delete and SCell release"

[End CNI-127108]

UEs stay in the “pre-scheduler candidate set” until their resource request has been served (5G_L2_226), or the UE is no longer eligible for scheduling, e.g., due to one of the exceptions mentioned above. Note: UE may have more than one resource requests, only all its resource requests are served, UE is not added into “pre-scheduler candidate set”.

[Before CB012734-E]

At each PDSCH scheduling occasion, the pre-scheduler creates the “Candidate Set 1” (CS1) (5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the pre-scheduler candidate set.

[CB012734-E] At each PDSCH scheduling occasion,

- If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = False or rdActEnhBeamSelection = False, the pre-scheduler creates the “Candidate Set 1” (CS1) (5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the pre-scheduler candidate set.

 -Else, the pre-scheduler performs the beam selection as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_27542_replaced([11174581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and determines the set of UEs the selected beam serves to create the “Candidate Set 1” (CS1).

-End

[End CB012734-E]

For this set UEs are selected in the order of the pre-scheduler candidate set, i.e., in order of their request class priority (note: request class sub-priority is not considered). The pre-scheduler selects either up to rdMaxNumUeTdDl UEs (when CPU overload control is disabled) or up to schedulingCapacity UEs (when CPU overload control is enabled) from the pre-scheduler candidate set [Before CNI-127108](https://systeminsights.ext.net.nokia.com/5G_UP_ALG_4825_replaced([11195013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4tnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[CNI-127108](https://systeminsights.ext.net.nokia.com/5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CNI-127108]. For detail about CPU overload control, please refer to 5G_L2_1820.

---

#### 2.2.1.1.0-3 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs TD Scheduler overview (ID: 11147585)

**2.2.1.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147592`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs The Time Domain (TD) scheduler takes “Candidate Set 1” (CS1) as the input for TD scheduling decisions.

[Before CB012734-E]

In case of analog beamforming, the TD scheduler selects all UEs corresponding to the beam which is associated with the highest priority UE (5G_UP_ALG_4251_replaced([11175632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the “CS1 Selected” set (i.e. rrmDlCandidateSet1Selected of 5G_UP_ALG_4258_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Here priority considers both the priority class (5G_UP_ALG_9465_replaced([11174010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuXqrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), as well as the sub-priority of the priority class (5G_UP_ALG_4147_replaced([11174034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case multiple UEs have the same priority class, as described in 5G_L2_223.

[CB012734-E] In case of analog beamforming,

-If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = False or rdActEnhBeamSelection = False, the TD scheduler selects all UEs corresponding to the beam which is associated with the highest priority UE (5G_UP_ALG_4251_replaced([11175632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the “CS1 Selected” set (i.e. rrmDlCandidateSet1Selected of 5G_UP_ALG_4258_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Here priority considers both the priority class (5G_UP_ALG_9465_replaced([11174010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuXqrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), as well as the sub-priority of the priority class (5G_UP_ALG_4147_replaced([11174034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case multiple UEs have the same priority class, as described in 5G_L2_223.

-Else the selection of UEs corresponding to the beam associated with the highest priority UE is skipped as it's already performed in Pre-scheduler as described in 5G_UP_ALG_27542_replaced([11174581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). As a consequence, “CS1 Selected” is identical to "Candidate set 1".

-End.

[End CB012734-E]

In case of digital beamforming or if beamforming is not enabled, “CS1 Selected” is identical to CS1 (5G_UP_ALG_4258_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Based on “CS1 Selected”, the TD scheduler creates “Candidate Set 2” (CS2) (5G_UP_ALG_4257_replaced([11175678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is a set of carrier-specific UE list. CS2 is created on carrier (or cell) basis, that is, one and only one CS2 is created for each carrier (or cell). For FR1 (where only one carrier or cell is served by each DL Scheduler instance) or when CA is disabled (so only one serving cell is provisioned to UE always), for each element (or each UE) in “CS1 Selected”, the TD scheduler assigns this UE to appropriate CS2. For FR2 (where multiple carriers / cells may be served by each DL Scheduler instance) and when CA is enabled (so more than one serving cell may be provisioned to UE), a CA UE may be assigned to more than one CS2 according to the number of serving cells provisioned to it and the DL scheduling eligible status of each serving cell. Some UEs may be excluded due to carrier (or cell) based (rather than sub-cell based) physical resource availability checking or scheduling constraints, e.g. for the scenario specified in 5G_UP_ALG_9485_replaced([11175683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “DTX optimized specific CS1 UE handling”, 5G_UP_ALG_4263_replaced([11175793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kultHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Limit Scheduling Opportunities of UEs with few DRB Data in DL Buffer”, etc.

To distinguish the “to-be-scheduled UEs” set mentioned below which is subcell based, let’s call the CS2 created by now ‘CS2_candidate’, and call the “to-be-scheduled UEs” set mentioned below ‘CS2_tobescheduled’. When term ‘CS2’ without any postfix being referenced, it could mean to either ‘CS2_candidate’ or ‘CS2_tobescheduled’ depending on the text context referencing to it.

After CS2 has been determined on carrier basis, the TD scheduler builds the “to-be-scheduled UEs” set on sub-cell basis based on CS2 (5G_UP_ALG_4292_replaced([11177281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is called CS2_tobescheduled. For each “to-be-scheduled UEs” set, this set contains a list created by subsequently adding UEs in the same order of as CS2 building up to a maximum of rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl UEs in all BWPs (5G_UP_ALG_4302_replaced([11177392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuu3CfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rrmNumUesFdmDlInitialBWP in initial BWP (5G_UP_ALG_4304_replaced([11177413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuu3DfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), while ensuring there are sufficient resources available according to the Checks specified in 5G_UP_ALG_4297_replaced([11177362](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuu3A_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), supposing resources for SIB1 and SI messages (5G_UP_ALG_3747_replaced([11165240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktgH9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & 5G_UP_ALG_3800_replaced([11166015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and resources for Paging (5G_UP_ALG_4293_replaced([11177286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) have been excluded already.

FDM Scheduler are used to schedule multiple UEs in a single slot:

- FDM Scheduler is used for the scheduling of multiple UEs in a single slot by giving each UE different frequency resources.

- Mu MIMO scheduler is embedded in FDM scheduler.

Note: FDM Scheduler is only needed for FR1.

---

#### 2.2.1.1.0-4 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs SD Scheduler overview (ID: 11147599)

#### 2.2.2.2.0-4 Scheduling Sets UE reassignment from dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic to drbTraffic request class (ID: 11147777)

**2.2.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11147783`)

Scheduling Sets The conditions for the reassignment to drbTraffic request class are specified in 5G_L2_5938.

The PF metric is not reset upon this reassignment.

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-5 Scheduling Sets PUCCH tokens preallocation (ID: 11147789)

**2.2.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11147796`)

Scheduling Sets [CB008593-A] if the UE's startingPrb of perSrConfig for periodic SR is aligned with sharedSrPrb and actSharedSr is True in PsCell_CellSetupReq, and if the DL transmissions HARQ timing will overlap with the UE's F1 SR timing (no PUCCH F3 resource for the UE at the time), the PUCCH resource won't be allocated to the UE and the UE shall be skipped for DL transmission this time, even the UE is the only UE using sharedSrPrb for SR or the UE will have PUSCH transmission in this UL slot [End CB008593-A]

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-6 Scheduling Sets Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to HARQ-AN bit size restriction (ID: 11147802)

**2.2.2.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11147807`)

Scheduling Sets For CA UE with PUCCH allocated by DPA (Distributed PUCCH Allocation), in any serving cell, if cDai[Before PR704798] and tDai values were [PR704798] is [End PR704798] set to INVALID_VALUE during step 4 of the common algorithm of cDai/tDai/symbol0Restrict determination (see 5G_L2_8820_replaced([11158574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25LY2PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then this UE shall be removed from DL pre-scheduler Priority Lists for the given DL slot.

As PUCCH resource has already been allocated to UE by DPA, PM counter M55316CRD50005 (Number of CA UE blocked scheduling due to lack of PUCCH resource units, see 5G_UP_ALG_2958_replaced([11124049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be incremented.

CP2 Reference: 5G_UP_ALG_14878_replaced([11174430](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-7 Scheduling Sets Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to dropped K1 (ID: 11147814)

**2.2.2.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11147822`)

Scheduling Sets For CA UE attached to FR1 TDD PCell with long PUCCH, if K1 value of the PCell was dropped (see 5G_L2_8944_replaced([11156854](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO1_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then this UE shall be removed from DL pre-scheduler Priority Lists for the given DL slot.

CP2 Reference: 5G_UP_ALG_14929_replaced([11116229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-8 Scheduling Sets Calculating sum of scheduling weights based on Priority Lists (ID: 11147826)

**2.2.2.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11147834`)

Scheduling Sets If NRCELL.actEnhancedFlowControlETh = TRUE, the calculation of sumOfWeightsOverAllEligibleBearersOnCarrier(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_11650_replaced([11192708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is based on N UEs in drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class in CS1 list, and additional total of M UEs in the drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic piority list [PR739128]and L empty buffer UEs in UE context DB[End PR739128].

where

N + M [PR739128]+ L[End PR739128] <= rdMaxNumUeTdDl, as per 5G_UP_ALG_11650_replaced([11192708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

M <= number of UEs in drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic priority list;

[PR739128]L <= rdMaxEmptyBufferUeInSumOfWeights(refer to 5G_L2_16438_replaced([11182693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27d3w_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If the UE of eth is being calculated is an empty buffer UE, it shall be included as per 5G_UP_ALG_11650_replaced([11192708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR739128]

In the drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic piority list, additional UEs, which are following the UEs selected into CS1 list, are taken into account in the calculation of sumOfWeightsOverAllEligibleBearersOnCarrier: if N UEs from position x to position x+(N-1) are selected as per 5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), additional M UEs from position x+N to position x+N+(M-1) are considered.

Pre-build table (only applied for FR2) 11147865: Pre-build table (only applied for FR2) 11147865: Pre-build table (only applied for FR2) 11147865: Pre-build table (only applied for FR2) 11147865: Pre-build table (only applied for FR2) 11147865: Pre-build table (only applied for FR2) This requirement is only applied to FR2 [CB012734-A] and only when parameter actDedicatedCsiSlots, received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq, is not TRUE (i.e. FALSE or Absent) [End CB012734-A]. Background: The CPU performance is critical for FR2 especially in case of DL 8CC CA. DL TD scheduler take more time than expected so that it cause FD scheduler delay too much. So removing unnecessary handling in DL slot and moving them to UL slot could relieve the burden in DL slots effectively. Solution: The solution is introducing a pre-build table. 1.Content of pre-build table Array of beamSelectionForCsiOrSib: beamSelection result of SIB slot for next continous DL slots. Array of CsiSendReqInfo: CsiRsSendReq for the UEs which have periodical CSI RS configured in next continuous DL slots. 2.Procedure related to pre-build table Step1: Cell setup phase DL scheduler create a pre-build table for every cell when cell setup. Step2: UL slot 1.reset the pre-build table and initiate it by counting how many DL slots. 2.DL pre scheduler create CsiRsSendReq in advance which is corresponding to CSI RS configured in next continous DL slots and buffer them in pre-build table as CsiSendReqInfo. CsiRsSendReq for TRS CsiRsSendReq for UE specific CSI RS for channel measurement acquisition CsiRsSendReq for refine beam ( if exist ) 3.If it is the last slot of a frame ( UL slot ), check if SIB activation or not. SIB beam selection is determined when SIB activation. Then save the beam selection result in pre-build table. Step3: DL slot DL TD scheduler check and fetch buffered CsiRsSendReq from pre-build table and send out them to L1. DL TD scheduler get SIB beam selection result from pre-build table. Original performance result and idea is

Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access).</p>

### 2.2.2.4 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 (ID: 11147871)
#### 2.2.2.4.0-1 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 2.2.2.4.1 Beam Selection (ID: 11147876)

**2.2.2.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147882`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, L2PS shall select the selectedBeam in DL as per 5G_L2_13836_replaced([11147953](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWhfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.2.2.4.0-2 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 2.2.2.4.2 Beam Metric Computation (ID: 11147888)
##### 2.2.2.4.0-2.0-1 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 Beam Weight (ID: 11147894)

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147900`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, L2PS shall maintain the beamWeight in DL of each configured beam as below:

beamWeighti=sum(ueWeightk of all UE served by the beami)

With :

beamWeighti: the beam weight of the beamId i,

ueWeightk= sum(schedulWeight of all nonGBR bearers with non-empty buffer configured for the UEk), schedulWeight: the schedule weight for a non-GBR DRB reported in drbAddReqPs struct (5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The ueWeightk is updated each time the bufferBytes of one lcId goes from empty to non-empty and vice versa.

The beamWeighti is updated each time:

- ueWeightk of an UE already served by the beami is changed,

- A UE in beami, with ueWeight>0 becomes eligible/non eligible to be candidate for scheduling as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_4183_replaced([11174302](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuat9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- A UE performs a beam switch from/to beami

---

##### 2.2.2.4.0-2.0-2 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 rrmAvgBeamSchedRate (ID: 11147908)

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147912`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, the DL post-pre scheduler shall compute if needed*, the rrmAvgBeamSchedRate at the end of the slot, for all configured beams as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_27543_replaced([11174602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(*) The rrmAvgBeamSchedRate computation is needed in the case that at least one UE was scheduled over the PDSCH for nonGBR DRB traffic in the cellGroup, in the current DL data slot.

---

##### 2.2.2.4.0-2.0-3 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 Beam Metric (ID: 11147919)

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147925`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, the pre scheduler shall compute the beamMetric as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_27543_replaced([11174602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for all configured beams :

- Option1: at the end of the slot (in post-pre scheduler).

- Option2: at the beginning of the slot.

Note: In Option1, the eligibility criteria for UEs is not considered in the beamWeight computation(5G_L2_20093_replaced([11147894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NvevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

### 2.2.2.5 UEs selection for CS1 list (ID: 11147930)

[CB014044-A]- If NRBTS/NRCELL/actBestNList is set to DL or DL_UL, the NK list UEs shall be added into CS1 list, the algorithm see [12550648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Q5B2YyQrEfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), NK list definition see [12517582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_U2PXwBiDEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[End CB014044-A]

#### 2.2.2.5.0-2 UEs selection for CS1 list UEs selection for UEs in Pairing Group (ID: 12586255)

**2.2.2.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12586256`)

UEs selection for CS1 list ​​​when ZF_MU is enabled (actDlMuMimoEnh=True, actDlMuPairingGroup = True), aims to improve the zero forcing Mu paring possibility, 5G_L2_PS will use bucket algorithm for selecting UEs in DL paring group and prioritize the selecting UEs by put those UEs under a same sub-category in drb traffic ([11148498: Handling of DRB Traffic Request Class For NBR bearers](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24RZ0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

IF PG>=1 && N>=2

5G_L2_PS shall use bucket algorithm to select n UEs in PGs that with ZF_MU capability to prioritize to CS1 with request class as drbTraffic and sub-priority as subBandBfUeInPG , 2=< n =< N.

other UEs in PGs will be added to CS1 without checking ZF_MU capability with request case as drbTraffic and sub-priority as drbTraffic

ELSE

5G_L2_PS doesn't distinguish that in PG UE's ZF MU capability , and UE shall be selected using legacy algorithm ,( for legacy UEs' selection for cs1 [11147936: UEs selection for CS1 list](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWgvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1, n>= 2 , it means per step at least two ZF_MU eligible in a paring group shall be selected, or this paring group shall be skipped. IF all the paring Groups with less than two ZF_MU eligible UEs in per PG , then exit bucket algorithm.

2, PG=1, with or without using bucket algorithm to select ZF MU capability UE will have same result, but without updating bucket value.

where

-PG is number of pairing group

-N is room that in every step of bucket algorithm.

- ZF_MU capability see [12571009: ZF_Mu Candidate List](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m4HnYS8BEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

- request class and sub-priority see [11148498: Handling of DRB Traffic Request Class For NBR bearers](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24RZ0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

CP2 reference: [12447143: Bucket algorithm for selecting DL pairing groups](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EGVwwAmBEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

#### 2.2.2.5.0-3 UEs selection for CS1 list CS1list UEs selection Optimization for FR2 (ID: 11147953)

**2.2.2.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11147966`)

UEs selection for CS1 list [Before CB012734-E]

For FR2, when rdCs1CandidateUeNumCoeff>0, cs1List UEs selction optimization is enabled, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_23553_replaced([11193808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvvjtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rdCs1CandidateUeNumCoeff. In this case, for drbTraffic priority class UEs, following steps are optimized:

- To select max CS1Size number of UEs to Cs1List from pre-scheduler candidate set(5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the searched and inspected UE number can be much more than CS1Size when numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL greater then CS1Size, due to only CS1 eligible UE can be added to Cs1List. To limit the search UE number, for drbTraffic priority class UEs in pre-scheduler candidate set, only max maxCs1SearchNumber UEs will be searched and inspected.

 maxCs1SearchNumber = rdCs1CandidateUeNumCoeff * CS1Size

The CS1Size is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL is defined in 5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- For the drbTraffic priority class UEs, the cs1List UEs are chosen in a roundrobin manner, while the roundrobin start position shall only be moved for the slot when UlData_PucchReceiveReq has been sent and new PUCCH token become available. The move distance is the max number of drbTraffic prioirty UEs in cs1List of each slots of current HARQ window.

 Note that this cs1List UE selection optimizaiton is not applied to UEs with traffic priority higher than drbTraffic priority class.

Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012734-E]

In FR2, analog beam selection and UE selection for CS1 list is performed as follows:

Input Parameters

- actHighNumberOfUes (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- actPucchBeamConstraintFR2 (5G_L2_IF_3117_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- rdActEnhBeamSelection (5G_UP_ALG_27553_replaced([11193947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvxY0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Algorithm

If actHighNumberOfUes == TRUE And actPucchBeamConstraintFR2 == TRUE

Calculate pucchBeamIdList (Cf. 5G_UP_ALG_26785_replaced([11174828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If rdActEnhBeamSelection == TRUE

If siez of pucchBeamIdList ≥ 2

enforcedBeamList = pucchBeamIdList (with removal of duplicate if any, and sorted by beam metric)

Else

enforcedBeamList = empty

EndIf

selectedBeamId = invalid

cs1List = empty

maxNbrRntisInCs1List = max CS1 size computed by the Overload Controller

atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam= FALSE

If Slot with SIB And sibBeamId is configured

selectedBeamId = sibBeamId

EndIf

If selectedBeamId == invalid And Slot with Paging And pagingBeamId is configured

selectedBeamId = pagingBeamId

EndIf

Step1: Through highPrioClassRntis of priorityOrderRntis

Step2: Through drbTrafficClass Rntis is performed

Else

Legacy algorithm based on priorityOrderedRntis with PUCCH beamId constraint is performed (Cf. 5G_UP_ALG_26785_replaced([11174828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If UE is eligible (5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) And cs1ListSize < maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Add RNTI in cs1List

EndIf

EndIf

Else

Legacy algorithm based on priorityOrderedRntis is performed (Cf. 5G_UP_ALG_4101_replaced([11173728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuV1dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If UE is eligible (5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) And cs1ListSize < maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Add RNTI in cs1List

EndIf

EndIf

Step1: Through highPrioClassRntis of priorityOrderRntis

isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid = FALSE

For each DL High Prio Request class supported in FR2 (*)

Get the listOfRntis associated to the Request class

For each RNTI of the listOfRntis

If Request class == RACH msg2 (Cf. 5G_UP_ALG_26785_replaced([11174828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If selectedBeamId == invalid

selectedBeamId = ueBeamId

Attempt to add RNTI as in **

Else

isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid = TRUE

If ueBeamId == selectedBeamId

Attempt to add RNTI as in **

EndIf

EndIf

Else

If selectedBeamId == invalid

If enforcedBeamList is empty Or ueBeamId is included in enforcedBeamList

selectedBeamId = ueBeamId

Attempt to add RNTI as in **

EndIf

Else

isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid = TRUE

If ueBeamId == selectedBeamId

If enforcedBeamList is empty Or ueBeamId is included in enforcedBeamList

Attempt to add RNTI as in **

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

Until out of listOfRntis OR cs1ListSize == maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Until out of DL high prio request class list OR cs1ListSize == maxNbrRntisInCs1List

(**) Attempt to add RNTI:

If UE is eligible (5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Add RNTI in cs1List

atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam = TRUE

Else

If atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam == FALSE & isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid == FALSE

selectedBeamId = invalid

EndIf

EndIf

(*) Request classes handled in Step1 are all classes between rachMsg2 (included) to DRB traffic (excluded)

Step2: Through drbTrafficClass Rntis

If enforcedBeamList is empty

beamIds = sortedBeamIds

Else

beamIds = enforcedBeamList

EndIf

For each beam from beamIds

Get the listOfRntis associated to the beam

For each RNTI of the listOfRntis

If selectedBeamId == invalid

selectedBeamId = ueBeamId

Endif

If RNTI is eligible AND ueBeamId == selectedBeamId

Add RNTI to cs1List

atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam = TRUE

Else

If atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam == FALSE AND isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid == FALSE

selectedBeamId = invalid

Endif

Endid

Until out of listOfRntis OR cs1ListSize == maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Until out of beam list OR cs1ListSize == maxBnrRntisInCs1List

Output Parameters

- selectedBeamId

- cs1ListSelectedBeam

Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_27549_replaced([11174585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB012734-E]

---

### 2.2.2.6 Micro-DTX optimized scheduling (ID: 11147975)

**2.2.2.6.0-1**  (ID: `11147979`)

Micro-DTX optimized scheduling FA: gNB power saving

Document Owner: Fabienne Roosen (Nokia)

---

#### 2.2.2.6.0-2 Micro-DTX optimized scheduling Micro-DTX overview (ID: 11147986)

**2.2.2.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147993`)

Micro-DTX optimized scheduling The purpose of DTX optimized scheduling is to reduce the RU power consumption (that is not a linear function of the number of transmitted PRBs) by trying to bundle transmission of non-GBR data (excluding 5QI5) with the transmission of mandatory Physical Signals or Common Channels of a cell or with Delay sensitive SRB or DRB bearer(s) of same or different UE(s).

For this reason, a dtxMaxRetentionDelay delay applies to non-GBR data (excluding 5QI5) usually related to drbTraffic request class, CA activated UEs with at least one activated SCell being excluded by default. The UE is temporarily assigned to the dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class during this configurable retention delay. Then, UE is reassigned to the drbTraffic request class to schedule any remaining data.

[CB008238-F] In order to optimize the TCP slow start procedure or TCP connection opening phases (possibly including security), this configurable retention delay may only apply when all buffered data in 5G-L2-LO buffer(s) have been scheduled since less than dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling [End CB008238-F].

---

#### 2.2.2.6.1 Micro-DTX enabling (ID: 11147999)
##### 2.2.2.6.1.0-1 Micro-DTX enabling Enabling/Disabling of Micro-DTX (ID: 11148003)

**2.2.2.6.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148014`)

Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling 11148014: Micro-DTX enabling The Micro-DTX feature is enabled when actDtxOptimizedScheduler = True [CB008238-D] and the cell load is low.

To assess the load, 5G-L2-PS considers the ratio between the number of UEs in the CS1 list and the corresponding maximum number avgMaxNumUeCS1 (reduced in overload condition, refer to its definition in 5G_UP_ALG_8945_replaced([11174992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as described in 5G_UP_ALG_9949_replaced([11174961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

- The feature is disabled when the ratio is greater than or equal to rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdHigh_percent (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9388_replaced([11193368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvr5TfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- The feature is enabled when the ratio reaches a value lower than or equal to rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdLow_percent (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9463_replaced([11193377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvsgUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and remains lower than rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdHigh_percent during a predefined duration of rdDtxCellEnablingTimer_ms (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9390_replaced([11193387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvsgU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access).

Note: The processing of the cell load is part of the post-Pre scheduler and is only described here for the reader convenience.

[End CB008238-D].

The "Enabled" condition is only checked before assigning a DTX eligible UE to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic instead of drbTraffic request class as per 5G_L2_5933_replaced([11148047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9k_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Therefore, enabling or disabling of the feature does not impact UE already assigned to these classes until totalBufferednonGbrData returns to 0.

---

##### 2.2.2.6.1.0-2 Micro-DTX enabling Enabling/Disabling of Micro-DTX for CA active users (ID: 11148020)

**2.2.2.6.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11148034`)

Micro-DTX enabling [Before CB009333-C]

Although Micro-DTX feature does not officially apply to CA active UEs (with at least one activated SCell), rdDisableMicroDtxForCaUes (refer to 5G_L2_5932_replaced([11182433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27bbjPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) could be used to extend the feature to these UEs for test purpose:

[End CB009333-C]

- When [Before CB009333-C] rdDisableMicroDtxForCaUes = False [CB009333-C] caSupportEnabled (see 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True [End CB009333-C]

 CA active UEs are handled as standard UEs from Micro-DTX viewpoint.

- When Micro-DTX feature is enabled and [Before CB009333-C] rdDisableMicroDtxForCaUes = True [CB009333-C] caSupportEnabled (see 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = False [End CB009333-C]

 Already activated CA UEs cannot be assigned to the dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class (refer to 5G_L2_5933_replaced([11148047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9k_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and configured CA UEs shall be reassigned to the drbTraffic request class upon activation of its first SCell (refer to 5G_L2_5938_replaced([11148077](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9lvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The main reason is that CA active UEs have pre-defined scheduling opportunities on PDSCH slots selected earlier by PUCCH pre-allocation (DPA) and interworking study with DTX is not complete.

---

##### 2.2.2.6.1.0-3 Micro-DTX enabling Enabling/Disabling of Micro-DTX in overload state (ID: 12709808)

**2.2.2.6.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12709810`)

Micro-DTX enabling When Micro-DTX feature is enabled (see [11148003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and overload countermeasure for Micro-DTX features is active (see [11203944](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29-ZNfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11174974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

Then:
 5G-L2-PS shall take into account additional overload restrictions regarding enabling/disabling Micro-DTX described in [11174961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

request class when following conditions are fulfilled (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_8232_replaced([11174950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

- The Micro-DTX feature is enabled as per 5G_L2_5924_replaced([11148003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- The UE is not a CA UE with any active SCell (or Micro-DTX has been enabled as per 5G_L2_5926_replaced([11148020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for [Before CB009333-C] test purpose on [End CB009333-C] CA active UEs).

- For this UE, 5G-L2-PS has received a non-null BSR with dataAdded > 0 for non-GBR DRB (compatible with drbTraffic request class) in absence of previous data to transmit (TotalBufferedNonGbrData = 0)

Note: TotalBufferedNonGbrData is only an approximation of the data remaining in the L2-LO buffer; so the check on dataAdded helps 5G-L2-PS to exclude the UE from DTX optimized scheduling in case of presence of any leftover to transmit.

- if the [Before CB009333-A] NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling [CB009333-A] dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling (see note below) [End CB009333-A] parameter is greater than 0, the delay between the last scheduling which has emptied its associated 5G-L2-LO buffer(s) and the reception of new data shall be lower than this threshold (refer to 5G_L2_5903_replaced([11148230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24PkqvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 Then, dtxMaxRetentionDelay [CB009333-A] (see note below) [End CB009333-A] timer is started.

Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access).

If rdDtxMaxRetentionDelaySlotRounding is greater than one and lower than dtxMaxRetentionDelay, a rounding is applied to the slot number of the timer expiry. Although it reduces the retention delay and the bundling opportunities in a cell, it favors transmission in common slots in case several cells are sharing the same radio and may improve the Micro-DTX gain in absence of cell synchro mechanism.

In case of UE having several non-GBR eligible DRBs, reception of BSR for any of the DRBs is sufficient to enter in DTX optimized scheduling. [Before CB009333-A] TotalBufferedNonGbrData and dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer are handled jointly for all these DRBs. [CB009333-A] TotalBufferedNonGbrData is handled jointly for all these DRBs. dtxMaxRetentionDelay is DRB aware and handled separetly for every DRB. [End CB009333-A]

Notes:

- This assignment is part of BSR processing and only described here for the reader convenience.

- PM counters related to entry/exit are described in 5G_L2_5907_replaced([11192279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28i12_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB009333-A]

- dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- dtxMaxRetentionDelay is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxMaxRetentionDelay for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxMaxRetentionDelay (see. 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxMaxRetentionDelay (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB009333-A]

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-2 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling UE exit from DTX optimized scheduling (ID: 11148077)

**2.2.2.6.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11148096`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling If TotalBufferedNonGbrData of the UE returns to 0 before dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry thanks to co-scheduling (refer to 5G_L2_5951_replaced([11148333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24QLufvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this timer is stopped and the UE is no more assigned to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class.

Otherwise, on dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry [CB009333-A] for any bearer [End CB009333-A], UE is reassigned to drbTraffic request class to schedule remaining non-GBR data.

Refer to 5G_L2_5907_replaced([11192279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28i12_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for pegging of related PM counters.

When Micro-DTX feature is disabled for CA active UEs as per 5G_L2_5926_replaced([11148020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the first SCell of a UE is activated, a UE in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class is reassigned to drbTraffic request class and dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer is stopped.

Note that no reassignment takes place upon SCell deactivation of the last SCell.

[CB005788-B]

Note : UE's Data scheduling post DTX optimised scheduling may get delayed due to slot muting. An effect of slot muting could be such that UE's scheduling may or may not be delayed soon after its exit from from DTX optimized scheduling period (dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry or timer stopped). This additional delay depends on the conditions governing the slot muting deicions.

[End CB005788-B]

---

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-3 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling Typical scenarios: entry/exit (ID: 11148104)

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-4 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling delay handling (ID: 11148225)

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-1 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling delay handling - Pre scheduler part (ID: 11148230)

**2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11148249`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling Upon reception of new BSR non-gbr* DRB data

If Conditions to assign UE to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class are satisfied (refer to 5G_L2_5933_replaced([11148047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9k_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) And If

dtxDelaySincelastScheduling > 0 (see note below)

Check buffer of non-gbr* DRB data

If (totalBufferednonGbrData != 0) before reception of new BSR non-gbr* DRB data

No change compared with current implementation

UE stays in current request class (either drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic)

Else

Check rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling

If rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling == undefined

Means rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling is not significant

No change compared with current implementation

UE enters in drbTraffic request class

Else

numSlot = current Xsfn – rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling

If numSlot < (dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling converted in slot)

Means data received within dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling

Enter in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class

Start dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer

Else

Means data received outside dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling

Continue with current implementation to select the right request class (UE will enter in drbTraffic request class)

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

(*) non-gbr excluding 5QI5[CB008118-A]/69[End CB008118-A]

Notes:

dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-2 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling delay handling - Post-Pre scheduler part (ID: 11148256)

**2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11148262`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling After scheduling of non-gbr* DRB data

Check buffer of non-gbr* DRB data

If (totalBufferednonGbrData == 0)

rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling = current Xsfn

Else

rmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling = undefined

EndIf

(*) non-gbr excluding 5QI5

Note: This processing is part of Post-Pre scheduler (refer to 5G_L2_5992_replaced([11150839](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1MvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and is described here for the reader convenience.

---

Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access).</p>

---

#### 2.2.2.6.3 DTX optimized scheduling (ID: 11148333)
##### 2.2.2.6.3.0-1 DTX optimized scheduling Co-scheduling with Physical Signals or Common Channels of the cell or with Delay sensitive UEs (ID: 11148338)

**2.2.2.6.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11148352`)

DTX optimized scheduling There are two cases depending on the presence of UE(s) from request classes of higher priority than dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic (lowest priority) in CS1 list of current slot (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9471_replaced([11175687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

- In absence of higher priority UE(s), transmission of Physical Signals (SSB, CSI-RS for TRS) or Common Channels (SIB or Paging) may be required in this slot. UE(s) in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class could benefit from unused symbols or PRBs of the slot, so they are added to the empty CS1 list.

- In presence of higher priority UE(s), UEs in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class could be appended to the CS1 list for the same reason (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9471_replaced([11175687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Although PUCCH allocation for UE of higher priority is guaranteed, it was discovered in late phase of the specifications that a retransmission could be discarded when composing the CS2 list due to insufficient number of REs in special slot (will be addressed as part of CB008662 Adaptative retransmission). Thus, it may be that only DTX UE(s) with small amount of PRBs are scheduled (current implementation in Pre-scheduler before composing CS2 list has not been changed in late phase of specifications considering the impact versus gain).

If the [Before CB009333-A] NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling [CB009333-A] dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling (see note below) [End CB009333-A] parameter is greater than 0, in presence of UE(s) receiving non-GNR data outside the delay since last scheduling (in drbTraffic request class), UE(s) in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class could be co-scheduled with this(those) UE(s) in drbTraffic request class as specified above for CB008238-B.

Notes:

Co-scheduling with higher priority request classes of same UE is implicit as Pre-scheduler only considers the request class of a UE with highest priority (refer to 5G_L2_226_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In FD, allocated PRBs to this UE are distributed over request classes as per 5G_UP_ALG_4538_replaced([11185470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTexPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB009333-A]

dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G_L2_IF_1862_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB009333-A]

---

##### 2.2.2.6.3.0-2 DTX optimized scheduling Scheduling of Micro-DTX UE(s) able to fill up the slot (ID: 11148357)

##### 2.2.2.6.3.0-2.0-1 DTX optimized scheduling PRB threshold & CS1 threshold (ID: 11148364)

**2.2.2.6.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148369`)

DTX optimized scheduling If UE(s) in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class cannot be co-scheduled with other transmissions as per 5G_L2_5950_replaced([11148338](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24QLuvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS need to assess the occupancy rate of the slot for these users as per 5G_UP_ALG_9471_replaced([11175687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The calculation of PRB load per BWP is only required when:

- All UEs in the cs1 List are assigned to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic priority.

- The size of the CS1 list is less than to rdDtxCS1SizeThreshold (see 5G_UP_ALG_9392_replaced([11193397](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvsgVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Estimation of the number of available PRBs per dedicated DL BWP (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_8238_replaced([11175696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

The maximum numbers of available PRBs as per cell configuration, taking PRB blanking into account, are given by numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedPowerSavingDlBwp, numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedSmallDlBwp and numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedLargeDlBwp.

The numbers of available PRBs need to be adjusted according to the budget periodically granted to the cell by the BBRM of the PRB pooling feature.

Note that these numbers may not be a multiple of the standard RBG size of the corresponding DL BWP.

Estimation of UE cumulated PRB demand and PRB load ratio per dedicated DL BWP:

All dedicated DL BWP are nested and the PRB demand in a BWP contributes to the PRB demand in the larger ones:

PowerSavingDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ DedicatedSmallDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ DedicatedLargeDlBwp.

Low ends of each dedicated DL BWP are aligned on a common CRB (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1809_replaced([11110718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpHXNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) so corresponding CSS (Common Search Space) are mapped on a common PRB range with the same size as the CORESET(0) size, included in the smallest dedicated DL BWP.

Therefore, any UE that is granted with a DCI Format 1_0 into CSS of any dedicated BWP (transient phase of RRC reconfiguration) contributes to the PRB demand of the smallest BWP and larger ones with a granularity of one PRB.

Any other UE contributes to the PRB demand of its active BWP and larger ones with a granularity equal to the RBG size of its active BWP (the RBG on upper edge of the BW may be smaller than regular ones).

The PRB load ratio of a DL BWP is the ratio between the cumulated PRB demand across all UEs with corresponding active DL BWP and the number of available PRBs in this BWP.

The CS1 list content is emptied if the PRB load ratio is lower than NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxPrbThreshold in each configured dedicated DL BWP.

Detailed computation of cptPrbDemand[] and NbPrbAvailable[]:

nbPrbAvailable[powerSavingBwp]= numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedPowerSavingDlBwp

nbPrbAvailable[smallBwp] = numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedSmallDlBwp

nbPrbAvailable[largeBwp] = numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedLargeDlBwp

cptrPrbDemand[TransitionPhase] = 0; // Ues in transition phase processing

for ixBwp Є { powerSavingBwp, smallBwp, largeBwp}

{

if (actSlowPrbPooling() = true)

nbPrbAvailable[ixBwp] = min( nbPrbAvailable[ixBwp], cell.bbrm().numAllocCellPrbDl() )

cptrPrbDemand[ixBwp] = 0;

}

for each Ue[i] in cs1list

{

If (Ue[i].isUsingForceDCIFormat()= true)

cptrPrbDemand[TransitionPhase] += nbPrb(Ue[i])

else

{

for ixBwp Є { powerSavingBwp, smallBwp, largeBwp}

{

If ( ixBwp = index of active BWP of Ue[i])

cptrPrbDemand[ixBwp] += (nbPrb(Ue[i]) rounding to upper multiple of RbgSize of this Bwp)

}

}

}

if ( actPowerSavingBwp == true)

{

cptrPrbDemand[powerSavingBwp] += cptrPrbDemand[TransitionPhase];

}

cprtPrbdemand[smallBwp] += cptrPrbDemand[powerSavingBwp];

cptrPrbdemand[largeBwp] += cptrPrbdemand[smallBwp];

if (cptrPrb[powerSavingBwp] >= dtxPrbThreshold *nbPrbAvailable[powerSavingBwp]/100) or (cptrPrb[smallBwp] >= dtxPrbThreshold *nbPrbAvailable[smallBwp]/100) or (cptrPrb[largBwp] > = dtxPrbThreshold *nbPrbAvailable[largeBwp]/100)

{

All Ues stays in CS1List (nothing to do)

}

Else

{

Cs1List will be emptied

}

Note: this has been implemented as part of Pre-scheduler for simplification purpose considering initial requirements.

Note: if actPowerSavingBwp = FALSE, numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedPowerSavingDlBwp = numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedLargeDlBwp

if actMultipleDedicatedBWPs = FALSE, smallBwp = largeBwp.

---

### 2.2.2.7 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature (ID: 11148466)

### 2.2.2.7-1 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature Handling of DRB Traffic Request Class For NBR bearers (ID: 11148498)

**2.2.2.7-1.0-5**  (ID: `13447338`)

Slot blanking due to RF high temperature The TD scheduler shall determine the set of UEs that require the first transmission of DRB data(including NBR in case of NBR bearer). DRB traffic resource request class has two sub categories: CP2 reference : 5G_UP_ALG_4178_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If NRCELL.actNbrForNonGbrBearers = TRUE or NRCELL.actLargeBufferUe , DRB Traffic class shall be further subcategorized as NBR category, subBandBfUeInPG, LargeBufferUe and normal nonGBR category. To facilitate this subcategorization L2-PS software shall add additional priority index nbrDrbTraffic(in addition to existing drbTraffic) to account for NBR category. drbTraffic, subBandBfUeInPG, LargeBufferUe and nbrDrbTraffic shall be under DRB Traffic class. The following table gives the corelation between resource request class and priority index.

The above CP2 requirement will be implemented in L2PS SW as two seperate priority index values that shall be used to differentiate DRB bearer (NBR and Drb/normal non GBR bearer). This priority indexes are still under same drbTraffic resource request class.

As mentioned in requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4178_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) TD scheduler shall determine the set of UEs that require first transmission of data(in this case NBR bearer) if there is pending data in DL buffer.

           **** **** ******** [](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

| | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Resource Request Class | Priority Index | Priority IndexValue**** |
| rachMsg2 | rachMsg2 | 0 |
| harqTransMsg4 | harqRetxMsg4 | 1 |
| [CB015279-A] pdcchOrder [End CB015279-A] | [CB015279-A] pdcchOrder [End CB015279-A] | Below Priority Index Value is increased by 1 in order, start from 0 - rachMsg2. Note that one Resource Request Class” defined in 5G_UP_ALG_9891_replaced(11174018) may mapping to multiple Priority Indexs. |

#### 2.2.2.7.0-1 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature Priority handling for slot blanking (ID: 11148470)

**2.2.2.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148478`)

Slot blanking due to RF high temperature The definition of " Priority traffic " is as indicated in 5G_UP_ALG_18294_replaced([11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Also means " non-Priority traffic " is everything else which is not listed in 5G_UP_ALG_18294_replaced([11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Priority handling is applied as per 5G_UP_ALG_18285_replaced([11175107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) such that if the current slot contains scheduling requests for Priority traffic, L2-PS shall consider the slot as ' non-mutable ' and proceed with normal scheduling of DL traffic on PDSCH.

Otherwise if there is no presence of priority traffic and all the scheduling request is only for non-priority traffic, then the slot becomes eligible for muting. If the other conditions mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_18285_replaced([11175107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are also fulfilled, then the slot is muted and no data on PDSCH is scheduled.

Note :

1. If the current slot has the mix of priority and non-priority traffic scheduling request, then slot is non-mutable and hence no restriction imposed on scheduling.

---

#### 2.2.2.7.0-2 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature Priority mapping for slot blanking (ID: 11148485)

**2.2.2.7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12745486`)

Slot blanking due to RF high temperature L2-PS shall compute priorty and subpriority for UE data as per 5G_L2_223_replaced([11147688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24MhWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). As indicated in 5G_UP_ALG_18294_replaced([11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for single and multi-cell cases whever applicable, the priority traffic can be classified into below mentioned categories.

Non-UE specific traffic : SSB/refinement beam, SIB1, OSI, Paging, CSI-RS, TRS, RIM-RS

UE specific traffic : RACH MSG2/MSG4, HARQ retransmission, MAC CE, DL SRB data, GBR, Voip

Note :

1. GBR includes Voip traffic. Hence Voip traffic is always considered as priority traffic from slot muting point of view. Follow allowGbrForSlotMuting configuration to treat GBR and Voip as priority or non-priority traffic for slot muting purposes.

2. deprioritizedVoip and deprioritizedGBR are always considered as non-priority traffic from slot muting point of view

3. All types of CSI-RS is considered as priority traffic from slot muting point of view

4. Paging with Short message is considered as non-Priority traffic since it uses only PDCCH resources (does not use PDSCH resources). Refer 5G_UP_267_replaced([11348157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubS9xvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

5. RACH messages[04800820](https://systeminsights.ext.net.nokia.com/Check%20next%20point%20to%20know%20the%20priority%20of%20RACH%20messages%20Msg2/Msg4) [End 04800820], HARQ retransmissions, DL SRB data are not considered as priority traffic for Multi-cell case. This in combination with allowGbrMutingForRfCooling = false creates a priority inversion condition such that GBR traffic is prioritized over these traffic for slot muting purposes. Its recommended to keep allowGbrMutingForRfCooling = true in multi-cell cases but its still a valid configuration with allowGbrMutingForRfCooling = false resulting in RACH messages, HARQ retransmissions, DL SRB data getting deprioritized over GBR for slot muting.

[04800820]

1. RACH messages Msg2/Msg4 are indicated as priority traffic for multi cell case as per [11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_KI7Z4fvOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). However L2-PS uses an RnD parameter 'rdProritizeRachMsg2Msg4' (Refer [12744547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_2MgiAH0iEfCiUemk-K-C4g)) to further decide the priority as indicated below

 rdProritizeRachMsg2Msg4 = 1 (true) -> Implies that RACH messages Msg2/Msg4 are treated as priority traffic

rdProritizeRachMsg2Msg4 = 0 (false) -> Implies that RACH messages Msg2/Msg4 are treated as non-priority traffic

[End 04800820]

---

## 2.2.3 TD Scheduler (ID: 11148519)

**2.2.3.0-1**  (ID: `11148526`)

TD Scheduler FA: [Internal Domain] TD-Scheduler

Document Owner: TBD (KRK)

---

### 2.2.3.1 Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL (ID: 11148532)
#### 2.2.3.1.0-1 Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL Updating the average 5G UE DL Data Rate (ID: 11148538)

**2.2.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11148557`)

Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL L2-PS SW shall calculate rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i,t] for a given UE i following the procedure described below:

- When the DL TD-Scheduler has to calculate the PF metric for the UE and serving cell i.e. UE is a candidate with priority drbTraffic [CB008238-A] or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic [End CB008238-A] in the serving cell, it first checks whether rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i, t-1] has to be updated by either a (re-)initialization or by an aging. In which cases either of these operations is required is specified in 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 IF( (re-)initialization is required )

{

rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i, t-1] = rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i, 0], where rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i, 0] is calculated as per formula in 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated = rrmScheduledXSfn - 1;

}

ELSE

{

rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i, t-1] is aged using the formula in 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with: rrmNumSlotSinceLastDlSched = (rrmScheduledXSfn - 1 - rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated) and rrmDlSumOfTransportBlockSize = 0;

rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated = rrmScheduledXSfn - 1;

}

Note: If the re-initialization due to rdAvgDataRateReinitProhibitTimer doesn’t kicks in (because the time when UE has no data in any DRB buffer was shorter than rdAvgDataRateReinitProhibitTimer), rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot is aged considering also the time when UE has no data in any DRB buffer. This deviation from 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shouldn’t have a negative impact on the fairness as this time is anyway short.

- At the end of the scheduling process:

 IF(the UE has been scheduled with priority drbTraffic [CB008238-A] or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic [End CB008238-A] in any DL serving cell)

{

rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlot[i, t] is updated using the formula in 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with: rrmNumSlotSinceLastDlSched = 1 and rrmDlSumOfTransportBlockSize calculated as sum of the TBSs allocated to the UE for new transmissions in the current TTI;

rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated = rrmScheduledXSfn;

}

where rrmScheduledXSfn is the extended SFN (SFN * Nslotsframe,μ + slot) under consideration for scheduling. Nslotsframe,μ is the number of slots in one radio frame (see table 4.3.2-1 in 38.211).

Above processing is also applicable accordingly with multi DRBs on the UE, in the case that new DL BSR indicates BS change to BS > 0 for one or several DRBs.

- When one or several DRBs are added to or are deleted from the UE the PF Metric in 5G_UP_ALG_4232_replaced([11175151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the average DL data rate according to 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are processed as described above.

- When one or several DRBs with different scheduling weights are added to or are deleted from the UE the PF Metric in 5G_UP_ALG_4232_replaced([11175151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the average DL data rate in 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are processed above.

Note: In case of activation of non-GBR service differentiation during run-time of a UE existing bearers keep their existing scheduling weights, only new bearers will be setup with new weights. The new bearers enter the above calculations with their new weights provided in bearer setup procedure.

---

#### 2.2.3.1.0-2 Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL Updating the average 5G UE DL Data Rate for Power Saving BWP switch (ID: 11148565)

**2.2.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11148572`)

Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL [Before CNI-73045]

L2-PS measures the Average DL Data rate for the UE as per 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It also is updated when UE enters CandidateSet1 list during PF Metric Calculation in TD Scheduler which takes into account the aging calculation and reduces average DL data rate. This is done based on gap between the current Slot and the last slot when it was scheduled.

During the measurement measurementDurationPsBwp period for BWP switch between larger and PS BWPs, accumulate the Average DL data rate values when the UE gets scheduled and calculate the average DL throughout at the end of measurementDurationPsBwp period. This DL throughput is to be used for evaluation purpose to consider the UE to be eligible for a BWP switch. The average throughput calculation is done by taking into account average of average Dl data rate. This is computed without considering the aging factor, which implies that we apply previous dl data rate to unscheduled slots to increase sample size. At the end of each measurement period, this value is reset and new average of average value is computed which will be used in the current measurement period.

[CNI-73045]

Average DL Data rate rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForBwpSwitch for BWP switch is computed as per 5G_UP_ALG_1874_replaced([11111241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLop_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) only when the UE's scheduling class is in DRB priority.

[End CNI-73045]

---

### 2.2.3.2 UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account (ID: 11148578)
#### 2.2.3.2.0-1 UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account Skip of DL FD-Scheduling for Component Carriers in FR2 (ID: 11148585)

**2.2.3.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11148609`)

UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account In FR2, before starting the DL FD Scheduler processing for the next carrier, L2-PS shall check the remaining time till the end of the slot. If the time left is lower than a configured margin T, L2-PS shall drop the DL FD Scheduling for all the remaining CCs, i.e. nothing is scheduled on those carriers.

By doing this L2-PS shall furthermore guarantee that it’s not always the same CCs that are dropped.

The margin T [Before CNI-134375] is set to rdFdSchedLateThresholdFR2 (5G_L2_22738_replaced([11181877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XKGfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if DL FD scheduler is executed in DL scheduler EO (i.e. DL FD scheduler not run in a separate EO). It [End CNI-134375] is set to rdFdSchedLateThresholdForFdEo (5G_L2_22762_replaced([11181911](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if FD scheduler is run in a separate EO.

The main purpose of this is to prevent sending late DlData_ messages to L1-DL which, with current design, can get stuck if it receives late messages and cause a sleeping cell.

CP2 reference(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_4101_replaced([11173728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuV1dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) DL Scheduling of 5G UEs per L2 PS instance with traffic prioritization

---

#### 2.2.3.2.0-3 UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account Handling of DL Re-Transmissions requiring more PDSCH symbols than are available in the current slot (ID: 11148634)

**2.2.3.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11148653`)

UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account If the number of PDSCH symbols used in the initial transmission exceeds the number of available PDSCH symbols in the considered slot:

For a FDD cell which is shared with LTE and actLteNrDssLteCatM equals true:

UE is still allowed to be added to CS2 list.

For a FDD/TDD(FR1) cell and actAdaptiveReTxResMcs equals true:

UE is still allowed to be added to CS2 list.

For any other cases

then the re-transmission gets an invalid TD metric value ('Nothing to do' in L2-PS SW) leading to ignore that resource request for the current slot

[CNI-92005-23R2]

For the available PDSCH symbols determination, the mute of last sysmbol shall be considered for SSB slot in case of muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot !=0.

IF "muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot == 1(Muting of last DL symbol only in SSB slot 0)" AND "current is SSB slot 0" AND "no CsiRs in last sysmbol":

Last PDSCH symbol is muted and exclude from available PDSCH symbols.

ELSE IF "muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot == 2(Muting of last DL symbol in all SSB slots)" AND "current is SSB slot" AND "no CsiRs in last sysmbol":

Last PDSCH symbol is muted and exclude from available PDSCH symbols.

END

Note, muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot is NIDD parameter and received in PsCell_CellSetupReq, refer to 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CNI-92005-23R2]

- 5G_UP_ALG_4258_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Composing CS2 list

### 2.2.3.3 FR2 DL Event-based PF Metric Calculation (ID: 11148659)
#### 2.2.3.3.1 Overview (ID: 11148664)
##### 2.2.3.3.1.0-1 Overview Overview of event-based PF Metric calculation (ID: 11148671)

**2.2.3.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148678`)

Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview 11148678: Overview In order to further decrease the CPU cost in beam selection procedure when there are multiple UEs and multiple carriers for FR2, event-based PF metric calculation is introduced. Now for each UE in priority list with DRB priority class the PF metric will not be calculated in each DL slot any more as before, instead such UEs will only update PF metric with a relative ratio in idle slot, meanwhile for those UEs which have received the PF metric event, their PF metric would be calculated in the next DL slot based on current DL data rate, average DL data rate and UE scheduling weight. The PF metric events are those events triggered asynchronously which would impact DL UE data rate calculation, the description of each kind of specific event could refer to 5G_L2_13387_replaced([11148685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Sn8PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The UE DL average data rate will also need to be updated according to the relative ratio in idle slot or the slot when UE gets the DL grant. Following figure is an example of event-based PF metric calculation with 5GC001227 frame structure, assuming that currently there are three UEs in the priority list with DRB priority class:  UE-1  There’s no PF metric event triggered from slot 10 to slot 19, so PF metric will only be updated in idle slot with *relative ratio and *last updated PF metric.**  UE-2  There’s one PF metric event triggered in slot 11, so in next DL slot the PF metric is calculated based on DL data rate and UE scheduling weight, then in UL slot 14 the PF metric is updated with PF metric of slot 2 and *relative ratio.*  UE-3  There is no PF metric event triggered from slot 10 to 13, so in UL slot 14 PF metric is updated with *last updated PF metric and *relative ratio. In slot 16, UE gets DL grant, then the average DL data rate will be updated in post scheduler and then one PF metric event will be triggered, so in slot 17 PF metric calculation will be done due to event, in UL slot 19 the PF metric is updated with PF metric of slot 17 and *relative ratio.***

Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access). Link to "Event-based PF metric calculation": Note: 1) K is a R&D parameter as filter coefficient, the definition could refer to 5G_L2_1023_replaced([11181966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxK_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). 2) For the relative ratio used for PF metric and average data rate update, the binomial formula expression (1 – K) ^ N could use (1 – N * K) as approximation in implementation when K is a small value. 3) The idle slot in this paragraph means the slot in which the DL scheduler won’t do DL scheduling job. 4) For current DL data rate, average DL data rate, and TBS(Transport Block Size), the definition could refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4242_replaced([11175309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4243_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5) The UE scheduling weight could refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9885_replaced([11175183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuhbofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
