#### 2.2.3.3.2 PF Metric Calculation Trigger Events (ID: 11148685)
##### 2.2.3.3.2.0-1 PF Metric Calculation Trigger Events List of events that trigger PF Metric calculation (ID: 11148692)

**2.2.3.3.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148697`)

PF Metric Calculation Trigger Events FR2 DL PF Metric calculation is triggered by following event:

 BSR is received and traffic flow not suspended and bufferedBytes > 0;

 SCell handle activate decision with SCellActivationCmdType = DECISION_ACTIVATE_CMD;

 SCell process one CSI report periodic from Remote PCell,and csiType == cqiPmiRi;

 L2-PS process remote SCell CSI report on local PCell when new CsiRs Report is received;

 L2-PS process CQI report, If rd4x4MimoRAEnabled(See 5G_L2_1265_replaced([11186618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_277KwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) != 0 and rrmNumOfLayers is updated;

 Update average Ue data rate on scheduled Ues in post TD scheduler(See 5G_L2_7304_replaced([11150856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1NfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 2.2.3.3.3 Update PF Metric In Idle Slot (ID: 11148704)
##### 2.2.3.3.3.0-1 Update PF Metric In Idle Slot Update UE's DL PF metric in priority lists (ID: 11148712)

**2.2.3.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148717`)

Update PF Metric In Idle Slot If current slot is idle slot, FR2 TDD UE's DL PF metric and average data rate will be updated.

1, Update Relative Ratio

relative ratio = (1 – K) ^ slotNumber;

K is rdAvgDlUeDataRateFilterConst(See 5G_L2_1023_replaced([11181966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxK_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

slotNumber is number of slots since the last update of PF.

Note:

1) This relative ratio is used for DL average data rate update.

2) For the relative ratio, the formula expression (1 – K) ^ N could use (1 – N * K) as approximation in implementation when K is a small value.

2, Update Pf metric in priority list when no Scheduling

Loop all the UE in priority list, UE’s PF metric will be updated one by one based on last updated PF metric and an increased relative ratio.

increased relative ratio = 1/ (1 – K) ^ slotNumber;

K is rdAvgDlUeDataRateFilterConst(See 5G_L2_1023_replaced([11181966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxK_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))).

slotNumber is number of slots since the last update of PF.

Note:

For the increased relative ratio, the formula expression 1/(1- K) ^ N could use (1 + N * K) as approximation in implementation when K is a small value.

3, Reset relative ratio

Reset relative ratio to 0;

---

#### 2.2.3.3.4 PF Metric calculation triggered by PF metric event (ID: 11148725)
##### 2.2.3.3.4.0-1 PF Metric calculation triggered by PF metric event PF Metric Calculation (ID: 11148727)

**2.2.3.3.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11148739`)

PF Metric calculation triggered by PF metric event 1. When there are PF metric event triggered for UE, this UE will be recorded in PfMetricUpdateUes data structure.

2. In each DL slot, for those UEs which receive PF metric event and have DRB priority class, their PF metric will be calculated one by one based on the formula described in 5G_UP_ALG_4232_replaced([11175151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3. After PF metric calculation is done, all the UEs with PF metric event in PfMetricUpdateUes will be cleared.

4. The new updated PF metric will be stored and used for beam selection procedure as before.

[CB012734-D] If actHighNumberOfUEs is true and rdActSinglePfMetricPerUeOnLoad is true and totalActiveUeLoad >= rdSinglePfMetricPerUeThreshold then the PF metric is calculated only for PCell and the resulting value is stored for the PCell and each SCell, otherwise the PF metric is calculated for each serving cell (see 5G_UP_ALG_26820_replaced([11175784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kultG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB012734-D]

---

### 2.2.3.4 FDM scheduling (ID: 11148746)
#### 2.2.3.4.0-1 FDM scheduling Overview (ID: 11148752)

**2.2.3.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148756`)

FDM scheduling in FR1, FDM is used to improve capacity by:

1) Improve PRB allocation such as resource usage is adapted to traffic needs (ie instead of using all the band).

2) Introduce frequency multiplexing of multiple users.

The algorithm is composed of two main steps:

1) UE selection: this step is responsible of finding UEs with all conditions to be multiplexed in same slot.

2) Resource Allocation: this step is responsible of resource allocation/distribution to UEs selected in previous step.

---

#### 2.2.3.4.1 UE selection (ID: 11148763)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11148767`)

UE selection FDM UE selection is responsible of finding UEs with all conditions to be multiplexed in same slot as far as max number of UE to be scheduled per slot is not exceeded conditions are:

1) available PDSCH resource.

2) available subcell resource.

3) available PDCCH resource.

4) available PUCCH resource.

---

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-2 UE selection PDSCH availibility checking (ID: 11148772)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13134080`)

UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE selection 13134080: UE 13134080: UE selection Pdsch availability checking is done depending on type of scheduling.

For SRB, 5QI1/5**/65/66/69, retransmissions available PDSCH should ensure a certain amount of predefined resources. In that case not only availability is done but also reservation of these resources (assuming that all other checks ie PDCCH/PUCCH…are passed) ie I know how much I need and I have enough resource for UE. Then UE will continue other checks and UE will be given already at this step PDSCH resources that it is asking for (exact position is not decided just the amount of available PDSCH resource will be reduced by what was given for selected UE). If there is no enough resources to satisfy the UE or other checks fails then UE will not be selected and no reduction of PDSCH resource.**

In picture above it’s an example of UE selection for a BWP where UE in blue is SRB all other checks passed then the amount of available resource in white is not enough to select another UE in red. Red UE is SRB too and is asking more resources than available, so it’s not selected.

[CB014474-C]

If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True,

When a UE is High reliable capable, reserve resources for GBR bearer(not applicable for VoNR bearers) in FDM reservation phase based on [[12689358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4trMsVZeEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)].

When a UE is High reliable capable and if only MAC-CE need to be scheduled for the UE in the slot, minimum resource reservation (rdMinPrbForRat1AllocHrDrb) is not applied.

If the available PRB for scheduling is lesser than rdMinPrbForRat1AllocHrDrb , then the minimum resource reservation is not applied

Note: Minimum resource reservation (rdMinPrbForRat1AllocHrDrb) for a multi bearer High Reliable (HR) UE is applied per Transport Block though the HR UE may have multiple HRLA enabled DRB's or one HRLA enabled bearer and other bearers are non-HRLA enabled.

[End CB014474-C]

In other cases, initial transmission other than SRB or 5QI1/5**[CB008118-A]/65/66/69**[End CB008118-A] then there is no condition on minimum resources to allocate for UE. So, check consist of ensuring that there is at least one PDSCH resource to give if UE is selected. Exact amount of resource will be decided in resource allocation step.****

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, there is a special case in which we can only reserve the lastPartialRbg of a different size instead of a normal size rbg (even if it is available), due to layerPrb constraints.

In this case, we need to ensure that the UE for which the lastPartialRbg is reserved, is also scheduled.

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-3 UE selection L1-DL subcell availability checking enhancement for ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4 (ID: 11148807)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11148813`)

UE selection To carry out the L1-DL subcell availability checking as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_4306_replaced([11177427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for each CS2 UE candidate, L2-PS shall additionally taken UE’s DL beam type into consideration as listed below if dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4:

 For each X-Pol beam, UE selection can only happen with the same beam type, that is, either within SSB/refined beam or within PMI beam, but never between SSB/refined beam and PMI beam

 For the first UE selection per subcell per X-pol beam, UE is eligible for scheduling no matter it is SSB/refined beam based (i.e. rrmDlBeam::isPmiBeam == FALSE) or PMI beam based (i.e. rrmDlBeam::isPmiBeam == TRUE)

 For the following UE selection per subcell per X-pol beam, UE is only eligible when it has the same beam type as the first UE

 In case of default SSB/refined beam being used for PDCCH/PDSCH scheduling (see 5G_UP_ALG_3188_replaced([11139322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only primary SSB/refined beam (which is always the best beam) shall to be considered.

CP2 references: 5G_UP_ALG_4306_replaced([11177427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_4309_replaced([11177456](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-4 UE selection PDCCH availibility checking (ID: 11148818)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11148828`)

UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection 11148828: UE selection PDCCH availability checking is performed to ensure that there is enough available CCEs to carry the DL grant.

If UE is transmitting in initial BWP or it’s in transient phase the pdcchResourceManagerCommonBwp will be used to search available resource. If UE is transmitting in dedicated BWP the pdcchResourceManagerDedicatedBwp will be used to search available resource.

In case UE is in dedicated BWP the search of available resource is performed with search space type 1 and the corresponding AL. In case UE is in dedicated BWP the search of available resource is performed with search space type 3 or UeSpecific and the corresponding AL (AL can be dynamic ie depends of UE’s radio conditions).

Search space will point to the coreset associated to the BWP on which UE should be scheduled. CCEs are checked in the coreset at predefined position between startCCE and (StartCCE + AL). StartCCE is computed according to 5G_UP_ALG_4090_replaced([11170944](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBFWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and AL is defined according to req 5G_UP_ALG_4055_replaced([11170246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) UE search space according to 5G_UP_ALG_4036_replaced([11168496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktwmofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Once a PDDCH allocation is done in one coreset it should pre-empt CCEs in all coresets in same BWP or in other BWPs 5G_UP_ALG_4032_replaced([11169907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In picture bellow Pdcch resources were allocated in coreset0 (yellow) then resources that are will be marked as not available red will not be used in coreset1.

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-5 UE selection PUCCH availibility checking (ID: 11148833)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11148847`)

UE selection Pucch availability is performed only for DL. It ensure that there is available resources to carry the HARQ ACK of DL grant on PUCCH.

PUCCH resource is of size of 1 PRB to carry up to two ACKs (Format 0 for short PUCCH or Format1 for long PUCCH). For more than 2 ACKs PUCCH size should up to 16 PRBs (format 2 if short PUCCH or format 3 for long PUCCH).

PUCCH resources (up to 8 per Ue) are configured by CPRT at call setup (via RRC for UE and Ue setup for L2PS) configuration of resources contains : starting PRB, size and symbols ...

PUCCH allocator must find radio resources (among those configured for Ue) that are available ie are not already used by an other UE. If none of resources confugured for ue is available at current slot+K1 [CB008294-H]or current slot + K1 for Msg4 A/N (5G_L2_549_replaced([11156818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if 5G-L2-PS is scheduling Msg4 (RaState of UE is scheduleMsg4WithoutDlCcchData or scheduleMsg4WithDlCcchData)[End CB008294-H] then UE is not kept further in to_be_scheduled list.

PUCCH allocator should also consider upgrading of format if for example UE has already 2 Acks then 3rd Ack should be added which means that allocator must find F2 or F3 instead of F0 or F1.

PUCCH allocator manages also multiplexing of PUCCH for CSI report with Ack.

---

Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access).Procedures: 1.Update NBW = n * NBW - sum allocated PRBs of higher priority UEs, when select the UEs which priorities are higher than drbTraffic [Before CB014044-UPD003] and nbrTraffic [End CB014044-UPD003]. 2.Check the condition to apply high buffer UE prioritization: if number of unvisited Ues in CS2 List > [Before PR852235] Nsched - L [PR852235] 1 [ENDPR852235]and sum of RBest> NBW (ref step 2.1 and 2.2, NBW > 0), enable this algorithm for high buffer UE prioritization(set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = true), otherwise disable this algorithm. [Before CB014044-UPD002] 2.1 Sort Non-GBR UEs and NBR UEs in descending order of RBest in CS2 list. 2.2 Calculate sum of RBest of the Top (Nsched - L) UEs in CS2 list. [CB014044-UPD002]. 2.1 Sort drbTraffic UEs in descending order by their Pending buffer in CS2 list. 2.2 Calculate sum of RBest of the Top (Nsched *dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio) UEs in CS2 list. [End CB014044-UPD002]. 3.Begin to select High-buffer UE from CS2 list when this algorithm is enabled and [Before PR852235] L ≥ Nsched - Nsched* dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio. [PR852235] min( unvisited Ues UEs in ‘S’, Nsched – L).<= Nsched *dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio[ENDPR852235] 3.1 Select this UE as High-buffer UE if the current UE RBest > NBW / Nsched - L (note: NBW> 0), even if NRCELL.NRDLMUMIMO.actMuAwareTdSch is set to True, regardless of correlation for MU-MIMO UE . 3.2 End High buffer UE prioritization(set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = false) if there is no available resources(NBW = 0). 4.Add UE into To-be-scheduled list after Subcell/PDCCH/PDSCH/PUCCH Check are passed. update NBW= NBW- RBest. 5.End UE selection when L = Nsched or No available resources. where: NBW:the total available PRBs in current slot. n: n = 1 if NRCELL.actDlMuMimoEnh is set to FALSE, else NRCELL.actDlMuMimoEnh is set to True [Before PR857062] and NRCELL.NRDLMUMIMO.actMuAwareTdSch is set to False, n = rdChannelBwMultiplierDl (see [12657403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBIEwEkSEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[PR857062] n= NRCELL.channelBwMultiplierDl [End PR857062] Nsched:rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl, see [11179079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku3Z6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). L: number of selected UEs (include SIB/Paging) RBest:estimated PRBs required by UE, see [11181264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio: NIDD parameter, NRBTS.NRCELL.dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio. NOTE: high-buffer-UE could be a NBR UE or a non-GBR UE.

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-8 UE selection Slot-based allocations with DlInterferenceAvoidance (ID: 11149914)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11149921`)

UE selection When rdEnableTdIcic is enabled (see 5G_UP_ALG_30165_replaced([11194010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall perform slot-based allocations depending on the UE classification as either 'normal' or 'high performing' (as dpecified in 5G_UP_ALG_8432_replaced([11181306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HmvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Rules:

1) For a slot, if its corresponding bit in rdFirstDlSlot is set to 1 and in that slot if the sum of FD resource requirements of the 'normal' UEs is greater than or equal to rdResourceUtilizationThresholdFirstSlot (specified in 5G_UP_ALG_30168_replaced([11194030](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the available channel bandwidth, then 'high-performing' UEs, even if selected by the TD scheduler, shall not be allocated any FD resources. This restriction is only applicable for 'high-performing' UEs having an initial transmission.

2) For a slot, if its corresponding bit in rdFirstDlSlot is set to 0 and in that slot if the sum of FD resource requirements of the 'high-performing UEs' is greater than or equal to rdResourceUtilizationThresholdOtherSlots (specified in 5G_UP_ALG_30171_replaced([11194040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the available channel bandwidth, then 'normal' UEs, even if selected by the TD scheduler, shall not be allocated any FD resources. This is applicable for both initial and retransmission of normal performing UEs.

rdFirstDlSlot is R&D parameter specified in 5G_UP_ALG_30265_replaced([11194020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is a bitmap, with each bit representing a slot in a frame. Note: It is recommended that when rdEnableTdIcic is enabled, then only the bits corresponding to the first DL slot after an UL slot can be set to 1 in rdFirstDlSlot.

---

#### 2.2.3.4.2 Resources distribution (ID: 11148869)
##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-2 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots (Step4) (ID: 11149280)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149286`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots Step4 Remove RBGs due to power limitation

usableRbgNum = number of usable RBG from step3

usablePrbNum = count PRB number from usableRbgNum, firstUsableRbgSize and lastUsableRbgSize.

if SSB slot without TRS

[Before CB008940-B]

if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'false'

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = numPdschPrbInSsbSlots

Else

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,(numAllocCellPrb-numOfSsbPrb))

[CB008940-B]

if isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is equal to 'false' (Refer to 5G_L2_IF_14_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for this flag)

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = numPdschPrbInSsbSlots

Else

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,(numAllocCellPrb-numOfNonUsablePrbInSsbSlot))

if CRI based beam refinement is enabled

numOfNonUsablePrbInSsbSlot = numOfSsbPrb + csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB

Else

numOfNonUsablePrbInSsbSlot = numOfSsbPrb

endif

[End CB008940-B]

Each time when L2-PS scheduler distributes the PDSCH resource to a UE on the Ssbslot, L2-PS determine the min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,numAllocCellPrb). Where the numAllocCellPrb is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) by the slow pooling algorithm in 5G_UP_ALG_6500_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

endif

else if SSB slot with TRS

if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'false'

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min { numPdschPrbInSsbSlots, numPdschPrbnInTrsSlots }

Else

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots, numPdschPrbnInTrsSlots , (numAllocCellPrb-numOfSsbPrb))

endif

endif

endif

if usablePrbNum <= pdschPrbInSsbSlots

return the bitset of step3

else

ConfRbgNumOfPSize = floor(pdschPrbInSsbSlots/P)

ConfLastRbgSize = pdschPrbInSsbSlots – ConfRbgNumOfPSize * P

usableRbgNumOfPSize = usableRbgNum

minUsableRbgSize = min{ firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize }

maxUsableRbgSize = max{ firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize }

if minUsableRbgSize < P

-- usableRbgNumOfPSize

else

minUsableRbgSize = 0

endif

if maxUsableRbgSize < P

-- usableRbgNumOfPSize

else

maxUsableRbgSize = 0

endif

if usableRbgNumOfPSize > ConfRbgNumOfPSize

remove (usableRbgNumOfPSize – ConfRbgNumOfPSize) RBG with size of P, starting from around SSB and first remove RBG with size of P after SSB

usableRbgNumOfPSize = ConfRbgNumOfPSize

endif

if usableRbgNumOfPSize < ConfRbgNumOfPSize

ConfLastRbgSize = pdschPrbInSsbSlots – usableRbgNumOfPSize * P

endif

If ConfLastRbgSize >= (minUsableRbgSize + maxUsableRbgSize)

Do nothing

else if ConfLastRbgSize >= maxUsableRbgSize AND ConfLastRbgSize < (minUsableRbgSize + maxUsableRbgSize)

remove index of minUsableRbgSize, set bit position to not usable

minUsableRbgSize=0

else if ConfLastRbgSize >= minUsableRbgSize AND ConfLastRbgSize < maxUsableRbgSize

remove index of maxUsableRbgSize, set bit position to not usable

maxUsableRbgSize=0

else if ConfLastRbgSize < minUsableRbgSize

remove indexes of minUsableRbgSize and maxUsableRbgSize, set bit position to not usable

minUsableRbgSize=0

maxUsableRbgSize=0

endif

usablePrbNum = usableRbgNumOfPSize * P + minUsableRbgSize + maxUsableRbgSize

if usablePrbNum > pdschPrbInSsbSlots

warning log

set all bit to not usable, i.e. NO PDSCH PRB ALLOCATED in SSB SLOT.

endif

endif

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-3 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots (Step5) (ID: 11149292)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11149305`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots If the value of actPdschAllocAroundSsb is equal to 'True’, then L2-PS proceeds as follows:

If the RBGs blocked as part of Step4 (5G_L2_9467_replaced([11149280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEOPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) entirely obstructs all the RBGs in CORESET0, then:

[PR798504]

- RBGs blocked by the positions of SSB, PRB blanking and CSI-RS for beam refinement calculated in Step2 and Step3 (5G_L2_4520_replaced([11149113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEMvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) should remain unchanged.

[End PR798504]

- Shift the RBGs that are blocked above SSB to upper end of the largest BWP (which means full RBGs).

- Relocate the RBGs that are blocked below SSB to bottom end of the largest BWP.

Else

Return bitset from step4

Endif

Else

Return bitset from step4

endif

Rationale: If the PRBs within the CORESET0 are obstructed on SSB slots due to power limitation, it would restrict the available slots to schedule MSG2 on the initial BWP. Furthermore, if the obstructed PRBs entirely encompass a small or power-saving BWP, then the Physical Downlink Shared Channel (PDSCH) grants for User Equipment (UE) operating in those corresponding BWPs would not be granted.

Notes:

- actPdschAllocAroundSsb is contained in PsCell_CellSetupReq(5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq (5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-4 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots for multi BWP enabled (ID: 11149310)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11149317`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots If there are more than one dedicated BWP configured(actMultipleDedicatedBWPs is TRUE or actPowerSavingBwp is TRUE):

The calculation of PDSCH schedulable RBG in SSB slots is per BWP and based on 5G_L2_4520_replaced([11149113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEMvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_9467_replaced([11149280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEOPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In FDM scheduler when prepare holes for RBG can't be used in ssb slots, [before PR767921] only the largest dedicated BWP marked RBG [PR767921] all the RBGs (blanked or not) of the large BWP [End PR767921] need to be taken into calculation because other smaller BWPs range already covered by large dedicated BWP.

[PR767921] note: with blanking at low edge, first RBG[s] of large BWP is/are not used by PDSCH as first Prb is/are blanked. But for other BWPs, first RBG can be used by PDSCH because first RBG is partial and does not contain blanked Prb. so hole preparation algorith has to consider all RBGs (blanked or not) of the large BWP. [End PR767921]

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-5 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDCCH for PDSCH in SSB slots (ID: 11149321)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13388571`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots This part is for DSS specific case when actAsymmetricDss = false or when actAsymmetricDss = true and a coreset > 0 overlaps LTE shared area.

Since PDCCH symbol overlaps with first SSB symbol in DSS, PDCCH power shall be considered. Only static PDCCH is considered.

During cell setup procedure, numOfDciAtSsb which indicate how many DCIs can be supported by power excluding SSB.

AL equals to dciDedicatedAggregationLevel if rd742isPdcchPatternActivated = true or aggregationLevel if rd742isPdcchPatternActivated = false

numOfDciAtSsbByPower = numPdschPrbInSsbSlots / (AL * 6)

[CB007372-M]

When actAsymmetricDss = false

[End CB007372-M]

If AL = 2, numOfDciAtSsbByPower = numOfDciAtSsbByPower / 2 due to 3dB power boost for AL2

When actAsymmetricDss = false

Available CCEs in SSB slots (availCceNumInSsb) are all possible CCEs on first PBCH symbol (symbol position 2) in cell bandwidth excluding CCEs overlapping SSB.

When actAsymmetricDss = true

Available CCE number in SSB slots (availCceNumInSsb) includes all possible CCEs on first PBCH symbol (symbol position 2) in cell bandwidth excluding CCEs overlapping SSB along with all CCEs in NR dedicated area in occasions on symbols up to first PBCH symbol.

numOfDciAtSsbByCce = availCceNumInSsb / AL

numOfDciAtSsb = min{numOfDciAtSsbByPower, numOfDciAtSsbByCce}

numOfDciAtSsb > 0 shall be considered before scheduling PDSCH in SSB slots.

#### 2.2.5.1.2 PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots (ID: 11149335)
##### 2.2.5.1.2.0-1 PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots frequency resource of PDSCH scheduled by DCI format 1_1 in TRS slots (ID: 11149342)

**2.2.5.1.2.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11149382`)

PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots This part is to calculate frequency resource of PDSCH scheduled by DCI format 1_1 in TRS slots due to power limitation. After calculation, one bitmap of usable RBGs and the number of usable PRBs are found. Calculation is done once during Cell Setup procedure.

Only full band TRS resuorce configuration is supported.

Step1. Remove PRB blanking RBG(already implemented in 5GC002534-A 5G_L2_4520_replaced([11149113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEMvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

firstUsableRbgSize first RBG PRB number after removing PRB blanking or startPrb is not 0

lastUsableRbgSize second RBG PRB number after removing PRB blanking

Step2. Limit available RBG

[Before CB008940-B]

if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'false'

[CB008940-B]

if isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is equal to 'false' (Refer to 5G_L2_IF_14_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for this flag)

[End CB008940-B]

if numPdschPrbInTrsSlots >=BWP_size-PRB blanked RBG PRB number

All PRBs/RBGs after step1 are available for PDSCH scheduling.

else

numOfNonRbgSizePrb = numPdschPrbInTrsSlots % RBG

numOfRgbWithRbgSize = numPdschPrbInTrsSlots / RBG

If downlinkBwp.location = 0

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb < lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used

endif

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= lastUsableRbgSize

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

endif

Else(downlinkBwp.location > 0)

If firstUsableRbgSize < RBG AND lastUsableRbgSize <RBG

If firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize > RBG AND numOfRgbWithRbgSize >= 1 AND numOfNonRbgSizePrb + RBG >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize-1 RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= max(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize > lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= min(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize < lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Endif

Endif

Else if firstUsableRbgSize < RBG

If numOfNonRbgSizePrb < firstUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if lastUsableRbgSize < RBG

If numOfNonRbgSizePrb < lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

Endif

Endif

endif

else

if min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb) >= BWP_size-PRB blanked RBG PRB number

All PRBs/RBGs after step1 are available for PDSCH scheduling.

else

numOfNonRbgSizePrb = min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb) % RBG

numOfRgbWithRbgSize = min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb) / RBG

- Each time when L2-PS Sheduler distribute the PDSCH resource to a UE on the TRS slot, it determines the min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb).

- RBG is the RBG size,

- numAllocCellPrb is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) by the slow pooling algorithm in 5G_UP_ALG_6500_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If downlinkBwp.location = 0

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb < lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used

endif

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= lastUsableRbgSize

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

endif

Else(downlinkBwp.location > 0)

If firstUsableRbgSize < RBG AND lastUsableRbgSize <RBG

If firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize > RBG AND numOfRgbWithRbgSize >= 1 AND numOfNonRbgSizePrb + RBG >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize-1 RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= max(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize > lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= min(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize < lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Endif

Endif

Else if firstUsableRbgSize < RBG

If numOfNonRbgSizePrb < firstUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if lastUsableRbgSize < RBG

If numOfNonRbgSizePrb < lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

Endif

Endif

endif

endif

[CB007112-A] The above information mentioned in this requirement under isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive flag is applicable for Large Baseband Pooling (CB007112) also.[End CB007112-A]

---

##### 2.2.5.1.2.0-2 PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in TRS slots for multi BWP enabled (ID: 11149390)

**2.2.5.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149395`)

PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots If there are more than one dedicated BWP configured(actMultipleDedicatedBWPs is TRUE or actPowerSavingBwp is TRUE):

The calculation of PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots is per BWP and based on 5G_L2_4663_replaced([11149342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VrQ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In FDM scheduler when prepare holes for RBG can't be used in TRS slots, only the largest dedicated BWP marked RBG needs to be taken into calculation because other smaller BWPs range already covered by large dedicated BWP.

---

#### 2.2.5.1.3 PDSCH available RE for TRS slot (ID: 11149401)
##### 2.2.5.1.3.0-1 PDSCH available RE for TRS slot Number of TRS RE calculation (ID: 11149407)

**2.2.5.1.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12650509`)

PDSCH available RE for TRS slot This part is to calculate number of TRS RE within scheduled PDSCH PRBs for UE. Result will be filled in ***numRateMatchingRes *in L1Data_PdschSendReq.****

As agreed, both full band and sub band TRS supported(actSubTrsRateMatch set to true) when pooling feature enabled. Note: need to check TRS PRB overlap with PDSCH if not full band TRS.

According to 3GPP 38.214 5.1.6.1.1, TRS resources are configured only with desity 3, i.e. row1 in 38.211 table **7.4.1.5.3-1. So there are always 3 TRS REs per PRB per CSIRS resource for tracking in FR1.**

Store TRS resouce number per slot in SlotAttributes for TRS slots and SSB slots with TRS, naming *numOfTrsResource. Store TRS frequency position of all CSIRS resource for tracking, naming *trsFrequencyPosArray,. It would be array of size 4 by 14, i.e. 4 subcarriers and 14 OFDM symbols to indicate TRS RE position in slot with TRS if actSubTrsRateMatch is true, ZP CSIRS for TRS will configured to occupy whole bandwidth to TRS configured symbols to identify the whole symbols will not used for PDSCH scheduling**

numTrsRePerPrb = 12 * numOfTrsResource to indicate how many TRS RE in slot with TRS. *numOfTrsResource shall only consider TRS symbols and PRBs overlap with PDSCH*

If UE is actually scheduled with *numOfPrb which are overlapped with TRS, then numCsirsMappingRes **= *numTrsRePerPrb * numOfPrb **if******

rateMatchingOption to 1: RATE_MATCHING_CSIRS or 3: RATE_MATCHING_CSIRS_AND_DCI **only if PDSCH is overlapped with TRS,**

if actSubTrsRateMatch is true

rateMatchingOption will be set to 4: RATE_MATCH_SYMBOL if no PDCCH and PDSCH overlapped or 6:

RATE_MATCH_SYMBOL_AND_DCI if PDCCH overlapped with PDSCH for TRS slot.

Note: For TDD FR1 with 52 PRBs configuration CSIRS for tracking (or the bandwidth minus the blanked PRBs is greater than 52 PRBs), not all the BW is considered as the number of PRBs overlapped with PDSCH. More information in req 5G_UP_ALG_7557_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CNI-147211-A]**

if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is true and actTddCsirsOpt is true, the above algorithm shall be applicable as well in case of ecpri

**[End CNI-147211-A]**

---

#### 2.2.5.1.4 Number of overlapped RE between DL PTRS RE and TRS RE calculation (ID: 11149434)

**2.2.5.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11149439`)

Number of overlapped RE between DL PTRS RE and TRS RE calculation If DL PTRS is enabled and PTRS should be sent with PDSCH according to scheduled information, see 38.214 5.1.6.3.

This part is to calculate number of overlapped RE between DL PTRS and TRS resources if overlap happens. Reult will be decreased from numCsirsMappingRes.

Since only time density 1 of PTRS is considered and PTRS dlPtrsResElemOffset is hardcoded as 0 in current PTRS related implementation, PTRS RE postion in PRB would be 0 as well, naming ptrsRePosInPrb=0, see 5G_UP_IF_710_replaced([11504147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSlZjPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). RE would be considered overlapping if ptrsRePosInPrb is one of trsFrequencyPosArray per symbol.

Check all TRS resources frequency position which are stored in trsFrequencyPosArray with PTRS RE position, count overlapped number of RE per PRB as numReOverlapTrsAndPtrsInPrb.

Get PTRS frenquency density as ptrsFrequencyDensity,

Number of overlapped RE, naming numReOverlapTrsAndPtrs = numReOverlapTrsAndPtrsInPrb * ceil(numOfPrb / ptrsFrequencyDensity).

### 2.2.5.2 HARQ Processing (ID: 11149446)
#### 2.2.5.2.0-1 HARQ Processing Bookkeeping table for UCI evaluation (ID: 11149452)

**2.2.5.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11149463`)

HARQ Processing 5G-L2-PS shall maintain a bookkeeping table for each configured subcell, which record the relationship between each HARQ Ack bit in UCI and the carrier index, HARQ process and PDSCH SFN and slot number. This can be used to extract the HARQ Ack/Nack info from HARQ Ack code-book in UCI.

For each item in the table, the following is recorded:

UCI sfn and slot number;

Free indication;

Number of scheduled UE in One TTI; for each scheduled UE:

> RNTI;

> total number of ACK/NACK bits contained in UCI; for each ACK/NACK bit:

>> Carrier Index;

>> PDSCH SFN and slot number

>> Harq process number.

The index of each item in the table is calculated from the SFN and slot number of UCI.

And the length of the table should be long enough to make the HARQ process aging algorithm available (5G_L2_284_replaced([11149481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), e.g. the length of table could be 40 TTI.

When a UE is scheduled in DL, the related information shall be recorded in the bookkeeping table of its PCell. Before record the information in the table, 5G-L2-PS shall first check if the position of table is free, if it is not free, 5G-L2-PS shall release the HARQ process previously recorded in the position which is a similar behavior as HARQ process aging (refer to 5G_L2_284_replaced([11149481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and free the position.

If rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarq is true (5G_L2_1189_replaced([11181836](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XKEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the first two entries shall not be used as C-DAI is set to 3 (see 5G_UP_ALG_4466_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarq is not applied for PUCCH format 3.

[CNI-109641-G] The information related to the UE scheduled on a remote Scell, received in PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingInd, shall also be recorded in the bookkeeping table of its PCell, see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_460_replaced([11197147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf5AIfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CNI-109641-G]

When 5G-L2-PS receives HARQ information from UCI on PUCCH or UCI on PUSCH, 5G-L2-PS shall find the corresponding position of the table according to the physical UL channel receive time, and check if the RNTI in the table is same as the RNTI of PUCCH or PUSCH carrying the UCI.

If the RNTI is correct, 5G-L2-PS shall handle the HARQ feedback for the carrier, PDSCH SFN and slot number and HARQ process according to the table for each ACK/NACK bit, then free the position of table.

CP2 reference(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_18215_replaced([11187299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Handle HARQ Ack code-book for DL HARQ multiplexing ...

- 5G_UP_ALG_4595_replaced([11187331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Dynamic Long PUCCH Token Maintenance for UEs over P(S)Cell Scheduler

- 5G_UP_ALG_4598_replaced([11187352](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Dynamic Long PUCCH Token Maintenance for UEs over Scell Scheduler

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-2 HARQ Processing DL HARQ buffer indexing towards L2-LO (ID: 11149470)

**2.2.5.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149474`)

HARQ Processing For an initial DL HARQ transmission requested via LoCtrl_PduMuxReq 5G-L2-PS shall provide an unused (free) dlHarqBufferIndex defined in 5G_L2_1976_replaced([11217544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_ElavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The dlHarqBufferIndex is associated with the requested transport block and shall be used to address this transport block within 5G-L2-LO for any possibly following HARQ retransmission. Earliest by freeing the DL HARQ process the dlHarqBufferIndex can be considered free. 5G-L2-PS doesn’t have to inform 5G-L2-LO about releasing the HARQ process. Note, the management of dlHarqBufferIndex is left to implementation.

[5GC000526-A] For the artificial PDSCH load, there are no HARQ retransmissions; no HARQ buffer nor HARQ process aging are needed; dlHARQBufferIndex = 0 is always used.

CP2 references: 5G_UP_ALG_4528_replaced([11184139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) DL HARQ processing

See also: 5G_L2_1976_replaced([11217544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_ElavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G-L2-LO shall implement the DL HARQ Buffer for HARQ operation.

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-3 HARQ Processing Control of the DL HARQ Process Aging (ID: 11149481)

**2.2.5.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13389030`)

HARQ Processing An allocated DL HARQ Process is made available again (for a re-transmission or new transmission) after the HARQ feedback for the ongoing transmission is received from L1-DL (UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD). This requires that L2-PS handles the case that the L1-L2 message providing HARQ feedback gets lost (for whatever reason), to avoid keeping an HARQ Process indefinitely blocked.**If long PUCCH is configured then DL Harq feedback can be received by UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD too.**

The strategy below is followed:

- Each time that a new HARQ process is allocated (new transmission) or that an HARQ re-transmission is scheduled, L2-PS stamps the corresponding HARQ process i with the current time (tHARQtx(i)) and stores it in the HARQ database;

- When a new transmission has to be scheduled (no higher priority re-transmissions are pending) but no free HARQ Processes are available anymore, L2-PS checks for all the HARQ processes how long they have been waiting for the HARQ feedback; if they have been waiting longer than rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime_us, L2-PS assumes that the HARQ feedback got lost and behaves as in case of HARQ failure (5G_UP_ALG_4532_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

FOR(All the HARQ Processes i of the given UE and subcell)

IF( tcurrent - tHARQtx(i) > rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime_us ) THEN ‘behave as in case of HARQ failure (5G_UP_ALG_4532_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))’;

where:

- rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime_us = rdMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTimeSlots * 125us, for above 6GHz

- rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime_us = rdMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTimeSlots * 500us, for below 6GHz

rdMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTimeSlots is defined in 5G_L2_14299_replaced([11183412](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27jXVvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR868177]

For T+T UL CA, when symbol muting is needed, check if there are any HARQ processes which were allocated before the muting request. If ‘yes’, then increment failShortenSymbolHarqInUseCount. If failShortenSymbolHarqInUseCount is equal rdMaxNumFailShortenSymbolHarqInUse ([13389048](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QgBXEAMzEfGozuGzRUXHpg?oslc_config)) then release all HARQ processes which were allocated before muting request and set failShortenSymbolHarqInUseCount to 0.

[End PR868177]

For the artificial PDSCH load, there are no HARQ retransmissions; no HARQ buffer nor HARQ process aging are needed.

When an HARQ process is released due to HARQ aging, 5G-L2-PS shall obtain the PUCCH receiving time from the HARQ data transmission time. Then according to the PUCCH time, 5G-L2-PS shall free the item in the related position of PUCCH bookkeeping table (5G_L2_280_replaced([11149452](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSUvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-4 HARQ Processing Control of the DL HARQ Process Aging for Harq processes to be scheduled (ID: 11149496)

**2.2.5.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11149508`)

HARQ Processing rdMaxHarqTxWaitTimeSlots [CNI-109641-G], defined in 5G_L2_3930_replaced([11183427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27jXWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), [End CNI-109641-G] is the maximum number of Slots a HARQ Process can await its UE to be scheduled for new/re transmission.

After that Delay, the HARQ is released by a periodic garbage collector.

Its default value 300 is aligned on L1CapacityLimit and determined by features CB006667 and CB007859

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-5 HARQ Processing Control of the DL HARQ Process Aging for DL re-transmission blocking (ID: 11149515)

**2.2.5.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11149523`)

HARQ Processing A new timer per DL HARQ process ID is defined by rdPerHarqTxWaitSlots (refer to 5G_L2_22536_replaced([11183438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27jXXfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which shall be started when DL re-transmission is blocked due to lack of PDSCH symbols in case PDCCH symbols increasing.

When the blocked DL re-transmission is unblocked and gets scheduled again, the timer corresponding to this DL HARQ process shall be stopped if it's running.

When this timer expiry per HARQ process ID is detected, the corresponding HARQ re-transmission shall be discarded and HARQ shall be released.

The original transmission shall rely on the RLC re-transmission.

Note:

This is only applicable for DL of TDD FR1 and FDD.

---

**2.2.5.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11149535`)

HARQ Processing Reporting of number of DL Harq contexts from DL HARQ database per cellgroup is reported in PsCell_getResourceUsageResp 5G_L2_IF_1659_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 2.2.5.2.0-7 HARQ Processing Maximum number of DL HARQ transmissions (ID: 11149541)

**2.2.5.2.0-7.0-5**  (ID: `11149572`)

HARQ Processing 5G-L2-PS shall support maximum number of DL HARQ transmissions as described in 5G_UP_ALG_3428_replaced([11153485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksmwFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Msg4 and 5G_UP_ALG_4532_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for other PDSCH transmissions. [Before CNI-130361]unless rdHARQDisabled (see 5G_L2_1882_replaced([11183313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27iwQvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) equals '1'. In that case no retransmissions are done and 5G-L2-PS shall behave as if maxDlHarqTx, rdMaxDlHarqMsg4 (see 5G_UP_ALG_10801_replaced([11153242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksk66vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and maxDlHarqTxDrb (see 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) were equal to '1'.
