#### 2.2.5.2.0-8 HARQ Processing Scheduling of a retransmission (ID: 11149578)

**2.2.5.2.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11149592`)

HARQ Processing 5G-L2-PS shall follow requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4532_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to schedule a retransmission.

- If the adaptive re-transmission scheme is activated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to TRUE) and applied as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_11943_replaced([11184268](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvRCjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

- TBS shall be calculated, as described in 5G_UP_ALG_4621_replaced([11192057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kviITvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with the MCS of the initial transmission and conditions of the retransmissions (number of PRB, rank, number of DMRS symbols etc...).

If the retransmission TBS is equal to the initial transmission TBS, the initial MCS shall be used for to schedule the retransmission. If the retransmission TBS is different from the initial transmission TBS, a reserved MCS shall be used for the retransmission.

- If the adaptive re-transmission scheme is deactivated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to FALSE) or not applied as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_11943_replaced([11184268](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvRCjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

- If for a FDD cell actLteNrDssLteCatM is activated and there is rateMatching in the slot (TRS, ZP CSI-RS (CSI-IM), slot 0 or slot 5), the reservedMCS shall be used if the calculated coding rate is higher than 0.95.

**[Before CNI-136855-A] In - If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, reserved MCS can be applied for a retransmission if the number of PRBs is different than for the initial transmission, that is to say if the last RBG is used in the retransmission and not the initial transmission, or vice-versa. **[End CNI-136855-A]****

**[CNI-136855-A] If the NIDD parameter NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, **in case of TDD mode with TRS/SSB slots, if a retransmission of an initial transmission granted as a RAT1 or dynamicswitch RAT1 allocation is scheduled and the PRB granularity is greater than 1 PRB then L2-PS shall roundup the number of PRBs to the next PRB granularity and if the number of PRBs is different from the initial transmission then L2-PS shall apply reserved MSC for retransmission. Refer 5G_UP_ALG_23663_replaced([11177504](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **[End CNI-136855-A]******

**[CNI-136855-A] The same or different CDM group(s) without data as initial transmission; The different CDM group(s) without data can be used only when reserved MCS(refer to 5G_UP_IF_1897_replaced([11515718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tUO_Wvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) used in retransmission. Refer 5G_UP_ALG_4532_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_24656_replaced([11192358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvj9ePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **[End CNI-136855-A]****

**[CNI-136855-A] If NRBTS/NRCELL/actVoNRIncCodingGain is set to TRUE, then a VoNR UE scheduled for retransmission is eligible to get allocated number of PRBs greater than their initial transmission. The UE is scheduled for retransmission with reserved MCS (refer to 5G_UP_IF_1897_replaced([11515718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tUO_Wvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 3GPP 38.214, clause 5.1.3.1) . Refer 5G_UP_ALG_14946_replaced([11185337](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ****[End CNI-136855-A]******

**[CNI-136855-A] In case of scheduling of Transient phase UE using RAT1 in the initial BWP(coreset #0), if the number of RBs used in retransmission is not same as RBs in initial transmission, then reserved MCS shall be used to schedule the UE to avoid retransmission failure. Refer 5G_UP_ALG_4622_replaced([11192072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvivUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **[End CNI-136855-A]****

If reserved MCS is to be used, the selected reserved MCS shall be the one with the same modulation order as the initial MCS.

In any case, the TBS of the initial transmission is the TBS used to fill DlData_PdschSendReq.

**[CNI-136855-A] Note: - If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, reserved MCS usage is described in dedicated part, see 5G_L2_3197_replaced([11164814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25vZe_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **[End CNI-136855-A]****

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-9 HARQ Processing Scheduling of the retransmission in case of PDCCH symbol(s) sharing with PDSCH (ID: 11149597)

**2.2.5.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11149604`)

HARQ Processing 5G-L2-PS shall follow the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_25288_replaced([11183118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvH4nfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to schedule a retransmission with [Before PR766243] n=5 [End PR766243][PR766243] n=20 [End PR766243] slots.

 If retxPostponeCounter == 5 //the retransmission is being blocked for too long

Drop the retransmission and free the HARQ process.

 If retxPostponeCounter == 1...4 //there is the same number of symbols in the slot as in an initial transmission. Then 5G-L2-PS schedule a retransmission with the initial transmission MCS, PRBs and symbols and retxPostponeCounter=0.

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-10 HARQ Processing Blocked transmissions (ID: 11149612)

**2.2.5.2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11149616`)

HARQ Processing The scheduling of a UE could be blocked in the following cases, leading to a loss of the allocated PDSCH and PDCCH resources. The cases are the following:

- For a cell with actLteNrDssLteCatM activated and adaptiveRetx deactivated, retransmissions on slots with rate Matching for CsiRs or for Pbch are blocked if the number of resources in the retransmission slot is lower than the initial number of resources * rdDlRetransMinFraction / 100. rdDlRetransMinFraction is defined in 5G_L2_2907_replaced([11192014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28hAtfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- No Free Harq has been found to schedule an initial transmission, even after freeing too old Harq process as described in 5G_L2_284_replaced([11149481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_3936_replaced([11149496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- No valid SLIV (see 5G_UP_ALG_2373_replaced([11115215](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr--_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has been found

---

### 2.2.5.3 Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission (ID: 11149622)
#### 2.2.5.3.0-1 Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission Requesting Transport Block building from 5G-L2-LO (ID: 11149629)

**2.2.5.3.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `12750115`)

Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission 5G-L2-PS shall request the new to be built Transport Blocks (concerns initial HARQ transmissions only, excludes RA Msg2) by sending the message LoCtrl_PduMuxReq for each of them to 5G-L2-LO. See 5G_L2_IF_864_replaced([10984513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WAjr_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details. The DL MAC PDU assembly is described in 5G_L2_1960_replaced([11216443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2--exPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The Transport Block of RA msg2 is built by 5G-L2-PS (see 5G_L2_318_replaced([11149693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24XgefvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) without L2-LO involvement, therefore no LoCtrl_PduMuxReq is sent.

In case of above 6Ghz configuration 5G-L2-PS shall send the LoCtrl_PduMuxReq message with **sfnToL1 and slotToL1 corresponding to the slot for which L2-LO shall send DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to L1**.****

The IEs sfn and subframeNumber/NR-Slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air. Note, from them 5G-L1-Dl derives the start of the corresponding L1 buffer.

The IE tbStartOffset of LoCtrl_PduMuxReq represents the relative start offset of the TB within subcell’s L1 buffer (see 5G_L1_5G21A_79).

The IEs tbIndex & tbStartOffset are set according to 5G_L2_319_replaced([11149707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Xge_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The IE pdschPayloadTbSendReqAddress shall be set to the address where 5G-L2-LO shall send DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to (containing the built TB). This address is provided by DlData_AddressResp (see 5G_L1_5G21A_36).

If rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and the TB was not allocated to any logical channel (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability, 5G_UP_ALG_10510_replaced([11185475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTexfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data is 1, change the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data to 2, and recalculate the determined Transport Block size (5G_UP_ALG_6874_replaced([11192598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlypfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The IE tbSize shall be set to the determined Transport Block size.

The IE numOfRbs shall be set to the number of logical channels which have been allocated resources in 5G_UP_ALG_4543_replaced([11185517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTez_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SRBs or in 5G_UP_ALG_4550_replaced([11185672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUs7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DRBs.

However, if rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and no logical channel has been allocated DL TB resources (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability) then numOfRbs shall be set to 1.

The corresponding RB parameters are set like this:

amountBytes shall be set to the value determined in 5G_UP_ALG_4543_replaced([11185517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTez_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SRBs and in 5G_UP_ALG_4550_replaced([11185672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUs7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DRBs.

However, if rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and no logical channel has been allocated DL TB resources (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability) then amountBytes shall be set to tbSize less the size of MAC CEs to be included. L2-PS shall consider the 5G-MAC subheader size, given in 5G_L2_1970_replaced([11215653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-5mSPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and the MAC CE payload size, given in 5G_L2_1971_replaced([11215683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-5mTfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall set the isL2PsLChBufferEmpty IE according to the following condition:

- Shall be set to true, when the amount of data pending in 5G-L2-PS internal buffer for that logical channel before this allocation is greater than zero and less than or equal to the data being allocated (amountBytes), meaning the buffer is emptied with this allocation. The 'data pending in internal buffer' means logical channel buffer size after accounting for any previous allocations in the current slot
- Otherwise shall be set to false

 If the Transport Block contains SRB1 data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to 1 (corresponds to SRB1)

If the Transport Block contains SRB2 data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to 2 (corresponds to SRB2)

If the Transport Block contains SRB3 data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to 3 (corresponds to SRB3) and the corresponding IE amountBytes to tbSize.

If the Transport Block contains DRB data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to the value of this bearer

[Before CNI-157970] If rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and the TB was not allocated to any logical channel (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability, 5G_UP_ALG_10510_replaced([11185475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTexfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then the logicalChannelIdentity shall be set to one of UE’s logical channels set up (excluding 0). Note, in this case 5G-L2-LO adds only padding bits to the TB. [End CNI-157970]

If the Transport Block contains CCCH data (SRB0), 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to zero (corresponds to SRB0) and the corresponding IE amountBytes to IE sizeOfRrcMsg received in LoCtrl_CcchDataInd. See also 5G_UP_ALG_3453_replaced([11153402](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksmJBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

If the Transport Block contains the MAC CE for Contention Resolution Identity (CRI) (RA Msg4), then 5G-L2-PS shall set the IE ueCriMacCeAvail to true.

If the transmission of a TA command is pending, according to the decision taken by the UL Time Alignment Control (5G_UP_ALG_3303_replaced([11150011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksRY6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then IEs taMacCeAvail, taMacCeValue are set accordingly, otherwise they are both set to 0. Note: during the integration phase, the sending of DL MAC CE shall not be enabled (taMacCeAvail = 0) as long as it is not supported by the test UE.

If the Transmission Block contains a PDCCH TCI State Indication MAC CE as decided in (5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the IEs pdcchTciMacCeAvail shall be set to true.

The IE dlHarqBufferIndex shall be set as described in 5G_UP_ALG_4531_replaced([11184177](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE requestType shall be set to "TB build request".

The IE requestType should be set to "dummy TB build request" for the artificial PDSCH load generation. The values for some other elements are defined as below:

- The IEs ueCriMacCeAvail, taMacCeAvail and sCellActDeactMacCeAvail shall be set to “false”.
- numOfRbs, tbIndex, tbStartOffset, dlHarqBufferIndex shall be set to “0”.

 If the requestType is set to "TB build request" (request is not for artificial load generation) and actOptimizedFlowControl == OptimizedAllUe, L2-PS shall:

- store eTh values from request in Ue context as lastSentEth to be used in 5G_L2_10486_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
- (re-)start rdEthUpdateTimer (5G_UP_ALG_15747_replaced([11193522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvtucfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), **5G_L2_17329_replaced([11150910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1PvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

 When more than one MAC CE scheduled in one MAC PDU and the total size of all MAC CEs is bigger than MAC PDU size, the MAC CE should be multiplexed according to the following sequence:

1. TA MAC CE

2. Scell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE

3. PDCCH TCI State Indication MAC CE

The IE maxPdschPayloadSize shall be set to the value of IE maxPdschPayloadSize of DlData_AddressResp.

---

#### 2.2.5.3.0-2 Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission Requesting Transport Block retransmission from 5G-L2-LO (ID: 11149669)

**2.2.5.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11149680`)

Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission 5G-L2-PS shall request the HARQ retransmission of Transport Blocks (5G-MAC PDUs) by sending the message LoCtrl_PduMuxReq for each of them to 5G-L2-LO. See 5G_L2_IF_864_replaced([10984513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WAjr_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on the message.

The IEs sfn and subframeNumber/NR-Slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air. Note, from them 5G-L1-Dl derives the start of the corresponding L1 buffer.

The IE tbStartOffset of LoCtrl_PduMuxReq represents the relative start offset of the TB within subcell’s L1 buffer (see 5G_L1_5G21A_79).

The IEs tbIndex & tbStartOffset are set according to 5G_L2_319_replaced([11149707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Xge_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE pdschPayloadTbSendReqAddress shall be set to the address where 5G-L2-LO shall send DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to (containing the built TB). This address is provided by DlData_AddressResp (see 5G_L1_5G21A_36).

The IE tbSize shall be set to the value used in the corresponding initial HARQ transmission.

The IE requestType shall be set to "TB reTx request".

The IE dlHarqBufferIndex shall be set to the value used in the corresponding initial HARQ transmission.

5G-L2-PS doesn’t need to add information on included logical channels (by e.g. IE amountRbs = 0) or 5G-MAC CEs.

[CB012979-H] The IE maxPdschPayloadSize shall be set to the value of IE maxPdschPayloadSize of DlData_AddressResp. [End CB012979-H]

---

### 2.2.5.4 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission (ID: 11149687)
#### 2.2.5.4.0-1 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission Building Transport Block for RA Msg2 and Requesting PDSCH Payload Transmission from L1-DL (ID: 11149693)

**2.2.5.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11149700`)

Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission 5G-L2-PS shall build the Transport Block of RA Msg2 as described in 5G_L1L2_FLOW_177_replaced([11186242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be_oQ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (without L2-LO involvement).

5G-L2-PS shall request the transmission of the built RA Msg2 Transport Block by sending the message DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to 5G-L1-DL. See 5G_L1_5G21A_79 for details.

In case of above6GHz 5G-L2-PS shall send the DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message for RA Msg2 scheduled in NR-slot n in the beginning of the next NR-slot n+1, as depicted in 5G_L2_353_replaced([11151020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24gDUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). By this, the corresponding receive window of L1-DL (defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_132) is respected. Note, this isn't needed for below6Ghz configuration.

The IEs sfn and subframeNumber/NR-Slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air.

[Before PR527935]

The IE tbFragmentOffset is set to 0

The IE tbIndex is set to 0.

[End PR527935]

[PR527935] The IEs tbIndex & tbFragmentOffset are set according to 5G_L2_319_replaced([11149707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Xge_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR527935]

The IE tbFragmentSize is set to the Transport Block size (payload in bytes).

Note, the MSC related to the contention based RA procedure to be supported by the DL and UL schedulers is specified in 5G_L1L2_FLOW_183_replaced([11187006](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfDSqfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.2.5.4.0-2 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission Calculating tbIndex & tbStartOffset_bits (or tbStartOffset) for every transport block requested from L1-DL (ID: 11149707)

**2.2.5.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12806598`)

Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission For every TB to be requested from L1-DL, the following is calculated:

- The IE tbIndex is set to 0 for the first TB in slot and is incremented by 1 for every Transport block requested.

For the same TB, the same value is set in both LoCtrl_PduMuxReq & DlData_PdschSendReq messages.

For Paging Message (when L2PS sends DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq, see 5G_L2_824_replaced([11173540](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26b9DPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) the IE *tbIndex in DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq is set equal to *tbIndex in DlData_PdschSendReq.**

- The IE tbStartOffset*_bits is calculated as follows:*

*tbStartOffset_bits[i]= 32* [ ( TBStartOffset_bits[i-1] + tbSize_bits[i-1] ) DIV 32 + 1],*

where i represents the current TB and i-1 represents the previous TB & *TBStartOffset_bits[0]=0*

For the same TB, the IE *tbStartOffset in LoCtrl_PduMuxReq is set equal to the IE *tbStartOffset_bits in DlData_PdschSendReq**

For RA Msg2 (when L2PS sends DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq, see 5G_L2_318_replaced([11149693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24XgefvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the IE tbFragmentOffset in DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq is set equal to *tbStartOffset_bits in DlData_PdschSendReq

[CB013100-A-UPD004] If UE allocation is affected by FD-POLITE PRB widening loop (see [12533165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jm0A4Bw4EfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) IE tbStartOffset_bits shall be calculated based on final tbSize_bits value in the last successful FD-POLITE attempt. [End CB013100-A-UPD004]*

---

#### 2.2.5.4.0-3 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission Sending DlData_PdschSendReq (ID: 11149724)

**2.2.5.5.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `11149816`)

Monitoring of DL GBR Load for Radio admission Control (RAC) This requirement refers to 5G_UP_ALG_4517_replaced([11183148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when GBR Admission Control mode = 1

if isAny**DlPrbPoolingActive And **slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed **set to 'false'******

**avgGbrPrbLoad(T) =Floor [nPrb_used(T) / nPrb_usable(T)]; where:**

*nPrb_used(T) = number of PRBs assigned for PDSCH Transport blocks that include 5QI-1**[CB008118-A] and **65 and 66**[End CB008118-A] bearers, up to time instant T*******

*nPrb_usable(T) = number of PRBs usable by L2-PS for PDSCH for any DRB, up to time instant T (5G_UP_ALG_4517_replaced([11183148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))*

Else

(isAny**DlPrbPoolingActive is set to 'true' or **slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is set to 'true')****

If numAllocCellPrb = 0 (initialisation phase) then

**avgGbrPrbLoad(T) = 1**

Else

**avgGbrPrbLoad(T) =Floor [nPrb_used(T) / nPrb_usable(T)]; where:**

*nPrb_used(T) = number of PRBs assigned for PDSCH Transport blocks that include 5QI-1**[CB008118-A] and **65 and 66**[End CB008118-A] bearers, up to time instant T*******

If condition in 5G_UP_ALG_1815_replaced([11110819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) = TRUE (multipleBWP activated) then,

nPrb_usable(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)]

{ nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, smallestBWP] }

Note : this equation is valid for CPRI/eCPRI72-a case and also for eCPRI7-2e case

l

Else

nPrb_usable(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)] { nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, largestBWP] }

End (condition in 5G_UP_ALG_1815_replaced([11110819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) = TRUE)

Where

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling depends on the slotType:

if actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 set to 'false'

- If slotType = SSB Slot,without TRS

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInSsbSlots, numAllocCellPrbDL- numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB **)**

- if slotType = TRS Slot,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInTrsSlots**, numAllocCellPrbDL)**

if slotType = SSB slot with TRS,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numPdschPrbinSsbSlots), numAllocCellPrbDL- numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB **)**

Other:

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = numAllocCellPrbDL

with

- the numAllocCellPrbDl is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) by the slow pooling algorithm in 5G_L2_8953_replaced([11246445](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3CDA5_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and received from bbrm in internal::ResourceResp (5G_L2_8852_replaced([11243971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BzwXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- numOfSsbPrb = is the number of Prb used to do SSB in the slot

- SmallestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the smallest bandwidth of the cell, the Power Saving Bwp is not taken into account for the SmallestBWP.

- LargestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the Bandwidth of the cell or the largest Bandwidth if CB008917 is activated.

**- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB given in CellSetup/csiRsBeamMgmt (5G_L2_IF_113_replaced([10968876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if present in the configuration, set to 0 instead**

else if actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 set to 'true'

- If slotType = SSB Slot,without TRS

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,**bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp - numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB **)****

- if slotType = TRS Slot,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInTrsSlots**, bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp)**

if slotType = SSB slot with TRS,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numPdschPrbinSsbSlots), **bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp- numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB **)****

Other:

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = **bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp**

End If

with

- the **bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp (5G_UP_ALG_13416_replaced([11183252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvJGuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed using '**bbrmUsableCellPrb' given by the slow pooling algorithm every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) ( 5G_UP_ALG_12403_replaced([11213315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1k_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and received from bbrm in internal::ResourceResp (5G_L2_8852_replaced([11243971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BzwXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).****

- numOfSsbPrb = is the number of Prb used to do SSB in the slot

- SmallestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the smallest bandwidth of the cell, the Power Saving Bwp is not taken into account for the SmallestBWP.

- LargestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the Bandwidth of the cell or the largest Bandwidth if CB008917 is activated.

**- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB given in CellSetup/csiRsBeamMgmt (5G_L2_IF_113_replaced([10968876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if present in the configuration, set to 0 instead**

End (numAllocCellPrb = 0)

End (if isAny**DlPrbPoolingActive And **slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed **set to 'false' )******

---

#### 2.2.5.5.0-2 Monitoring of DL GBR Load for Radio admission Control (RAC) DL GBR PRB Load Monitoring for RAC case actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 set to 'true' (ID: 11149861)

**2.2.5.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149867`)

Monitoring of DL GBR Load for Radio admission Control (RAC) That requirement refers to 5G_UP_ALG_8168_replaced([11183175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

when GBR Admission Control mode = 2

[CB010513-B]

if isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is set to 'true' and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 set to 'true'

avgGbrPrbLoad(T) =Floor [nPrb_used(T) / nPrb_usable(T)]; where:

nPrb_used(T) = number of PRBs assigned for PDSCH Transport blocks that include 5QI bearers up to time instant T

nPrb_usable(T) = number of PRBs usable by L2-PS for PDSCH for any DRB, up to time instant T (5G_UP_ALG_4517_replaced([11183148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If numAllocCellPrb = 0 (initialisation phase) then

avgGbrPrbLoad(T) = 1

Else

avgGbrPrbLoad(T) =Floor [nPrb_used(T) / nPrb_usable(T)]; where:

nPrb_used(T) = number of PRBs assigned for PDSCH Transport blocks that include 5QI bearers up to time instant T

End

If condition in 5G_UP_ALG_1815_replaced([11110819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) = TRUE (multipleBWP activated) then,

nPrb_usable_1(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)]

{ nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, largestBWP] }

nPrb_usable_2(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)]

{ nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, smallestBWP] }

Else

nPrb_usable_1(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)] { nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k,

largestBWP] }End (condition in 5G_UP_ALG_1815_replaced([11110819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) = TRUE)

Where

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling depends on the slotType:

- If slotType = SSB Slot,without TRS

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp - numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB )

if slotType = TRS Slot,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInTrsSlots, bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp)

if slotType = SSB slot with TRS,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numPdschPrbinSsbSlots), bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp- numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB )

Other:

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp

End If

[End CB010513-B]

End

With

- the bbrmNumMaxPdschPrbForGbr_Bwp (5G_UP_ALG_13416_replaced([11183252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvJGuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed using 'bbrmUsableCellPrb' given by the slow pooling algorithm every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) ( 5G_UP_ALG_12403_replaced([11213315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1k_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and received from bbrm in internal::ResourceResp (5G_L2_8852_replaced([11243971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BzwXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- numOfSsbPrb = is the number of Prb used to do SSB in the slot

- SmallestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the smallest bandwidth of the cell, the Power Saving Bwp is not taken into account for the SmallestBWP.

- LargestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the Bandwidth of the cell or the largest Bandwidth if CB008917 is activated.

- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB given in CellSetup/csiRsBeamMgmt (5G_L2_IF_113_replaced([10968876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if present in the configuration, set to 0 instead

---

#### 2.2.5.5.0-3 Monitoring of DL GBR Load for Radio admission Control (RAC) DL GBR PRB Load Monitoring for RAC case actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 set to 'false' (ID: 11149823)

**2.2.5.5.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11149854`)

Monitoring of DL GBR Load for Radio admission Control (RAC) That requirement refers to 5G_UP_ALG_8168_replaced([11183175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

when GBR Admission Control mode = 2

if isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is set to 'false' [CB012605-C]and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is set to 'false'[End CB012605-C]

avgGbrPrbLoad(T) =Floor [nPrb_used(T) / nPrb_usable(T)]; where:

nPrb_used(T) = number of PRBs assigned for PDSCH Transport blocks that include 5QI bearers up to time instant T

nPrb_usable(T) = number of PRBs usable by L2-PS for PDSCH for any DRB, up to time instant T (5G_UP_ALG_4517_replaced([11183148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Else

If numAllocCellPrb = 0 (initialisation phase) then

avgGbrPrbLoad(T) = 1

Else

avgGbrPrbLoad(T) =Floor [nPrb_used(T) / nPrb_usable(T)]; where:

nPrb_used(T) = number of PRBs assigned for PDSCH Transport blocks that include 5QI bearers up to time instant T

If condition in 5G_UP_ALG_1815_replaced([11110819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) = TRUE (multipleBWP activated) then,

nPrb_usable_1(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)]

{ nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, largestBWP] }

nPrb_usable_2(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)]

{ nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, smallestBWP] }

[CB012605-E]

Note : this equation is valid for CPRI/eCPRI72-a case and also for eCPRI7-2e case

l[End CB012605-E]

Else

nPrb_usable_1(t) = sum[over all DL slots k since (T-1)] { nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k,

largestBWP] }End (condition in 5G_UP_ALG_1815_replaced([11110819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) = TRUE)

Where

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling depends on the slotType:

if actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 set to 'false'

- If slotType = SSB Slot,without TRS

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInSsbSlots, numAllocCellPrbDL- numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB )

- if slotType = TRS Slot,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (numPdschPrbInTrsSlots, numAllocCellPrbDL)

if slotType = SSB slot with TRS,

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = min (min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numPdschPrbinSsbSlots), numAllocCellPrbDL- numOfSsbPrb- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB )

Other:

nbPrbUsableWithPrbPooling [k, BWP] = numAllocCellPrbDL

End

End

With

- the numAllocCellPrbDl is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) by the slow pooling algorithm in 5G_L2_8953_replaced([11246445](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3CDA5_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and received from bbrm in internal::ResourceResp (5G_L2_8852_replaced([11243971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BzwXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- numOfSsbPrb = is the number of Prb used to do SSB in the slot

- SmallestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the smallest bandwidth of the cell, the Power Saving Bwp is not taken into account for the SmallestBWP.

- LargestBWP is the number of PRBs corresponding to the Bandwidth of the cell or the largest Bandwidth if CB008917 is activated.

- csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB given in CellSetup/csiRsBeamMgmt (5G_L2_IF_113_replaced([10968876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if present in the configuration, set to 0 instead

### 2.2.5.8 Configurable Artifical Load Generation (ID: 11149986)
#### 2.2.5.8.1 Configurable Artifical Load Generation over sector beam (ID: 11149992)
##### 2.2.5.8.1.0-1 Configurable Artifical Load Generation over sector beam Configurable Artificial Load Generation in PDSCH Including SSB and TRS slot (ID: 11149997)

**2.2.5.8.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11150008`)

Configurable Artifical Load Generation over sector beam when is actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to any value other than non-zero (see [Before CB010944-A] 5G_L2_IF_4010_replaced([10967345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTe_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB010944-A] 5G_L2_IF_111_replaced([10968847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBJPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB010944-A]), the artificial load in pdsch including SSB and TRS slot is generated when targetTotalLoadSectorBeam in PDSCH is not met in the slot. After resource allocation of all UEs in the slot, the total allocated PRB is calculated.

If the total allocated PRB is greater or equal to the targetTotalLoadSectorBeam then artifical load in pdsch is not generated else artificial load is generated (see 5G_UP_ALG_17662_replaced([11183987](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

However there may be instances where the artificial load is not generated even when targetTotalLoadSectorBeam is not met. (see 5G_UP_ALG_17660_replaced([11183966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The PM counters DL_PRB_ARTIFICIAL_LOAD , DL_SLOTS_ARTIFICIAL_LOAD , DL_SLOTS_BELOW_TGT_LOAD and TRS_SLOTS are updated based on the aritificial load criteria met.

The artificial load measurement settings including the parameter settings to L1 are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_17864_replaced([11183920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Most of the L2PS functionality for artificial load measurement settings are reused from legacy feature 5GC000526.

---

##### 2.2.5.8.1.0-2 Configurable Artifical Load Generation over sector beam Configurable Artificial Load Generation in PDCCH Including SSB and TRS slot (ID: 11150015)

**2.2.5.8.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150026`)

Configurable Artifical Load Generation over sector beam when is actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to value two or three (see [Before CB010944-A] 5G_L2_IF_4010_replaced([10967345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTe_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB010944-A] 5G_L2_IF_111_replaced([10968847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBJPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB010944-A]), the artificial load in pdcch including SSB and TRS slot is generated when targetTotalLoadSectorBeam in PDCCH is not met in the slot. The CCE capacity and the start CEE calculation for dummy pdcch is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_15362_replaced([11170018](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt7lyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_17433_replaced([11171141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBsZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). actConfDlInterferenceGen is coupled with feature actDlPaWarmUp feature and all pdcch measurement

settings are resued from this feature.

However there may be instances where the artificial load is not generated even when targetTotalLoadSectorBeam is not met. (see 5G_UP_ALG_17660_replaced([11183966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The PM counters DL_PRB_ARTIFICIAL_LOAD , DL_SLOTS_ARTIFICIAL_LOAD , DL_SLOTS_BELOW_TGT_LOAD and TRS_SLOTS are updated based on the aritificial

load criteria met.

The PDCCH transmission settings to L1 are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_17436_replaced([11171723](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 2.2.5.8.2.0-1 DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation (ID: 11150050)

**2.2.5.8.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12790371`)

DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation When PsCell_CellSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq (see 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message is received, [Before CB014301-AA] or when updated when cell's down tilt offset is changed, [CB014301-AA] or when online modification of beamset NIDD parameters in PsCell_BeamConfigUpdateReq 5G_L2_IF[12536044: PsCell_BeamConfigUpdateReq](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wLou8R9PEfCQJ5daVHVkgg) [End CB014301-AA] 5G-L2-PS shall access the artificialLoadInfo structure (see 5G_L2_IF_111_replaced([10968847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBJPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

2. slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed for 7-2a or **slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed for 7-2e is enabled (see 5G_L2_IF_14_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall calculate the PRB demand for artificial load generation for EMF validation, as specified in 5G_L2_18383_replaced([11174645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26luBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .**

##### 2.2.5.8.2.0-2 DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation Number of PRBs for DL artificial load generation for EMF validation when slow PRB pooling is enabled (ID: 11150069)

**2.2.5.8.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150084`)

DL artificial load generation for electromagnetic field validation When in the given cell:

1. DL artificial load generation for EMF validation is enabled, as specified in 5G_L2_18356_replaced([11150050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Z8s_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
2. AND slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed [CB010630-D]for 7-2a or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed for 7-2e [End Cb010630-D] is enabled (see 5G_L2_IF_14_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 5G-L2-PS shall guarantee that the total number of PRBs allocated in the given slot will not exceed the upper limit allocated by the PRB pooling algorithm. 5G-L2-PS shall apply the following operation on top of the calculation of number of PRBs for configurable DL artificial load generation specified in 5G_UP_ALG_17661_replaced([11183983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

[CB010630-D]

if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is TRUE

layerPRBsForArtificialLoadGeneration = min{ConfiguredLoadInLayerPRBForEmf - layerPRBConsumedByscheduledRealUEs, numAllocCellLayerPrbDl - layerPRBConsumedByscheduledRealUEs}

where:

. layerPRBsForArtificialLoadGeneration: Number of layer PRBs on which artificial load needs to be generated.

. ConfiguredLoadInLayerPRBForEmf : see 5G_UP_ALG_25717_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

. numAllocCellLayerPrbDl : total amount of usable DL layer PRB of the sub cell, received in PsInternal_ResourceResp message content (see 5G_L2_8852_replaced([11243971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BzwXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

. layerPRBConsumedByscheduledRealUEs : Number of layer PRBs consumed by real UEs.

else

[End CB010630-D]

PRBsForArtificialLoadGeneration = min{PRBsForArtificialLoadGeneration, numAllocCellPrbDl - PRBConsumedByscheduledRealUEs}

where:

- PRBsForArtificialLoadGeneration: see 5G_UP_ALG_17661_replaced([11183983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
- PRBConsumedByscheduledRealUEs: see 5G_UP_ALG_17661_replaced([11183983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
- numAllocCellPrbDl is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell, received in PsInternal_ResourceResp message content (see 5G_L2_8852_replaced([11243971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BzwXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Rationale:

5G-L2-PS shall not meet the PRB level configured with emfTotalTargetLoad (see 5G_L2_IF_111_replaced([10968847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBJPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when 5G-L2-PS:

1. sets numAllocCellPrb = 0 for the given cell, as specified in 5G_L2_4109_replaced([11174562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26lG8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. limits the minimum stream-PRBs for DL artificial load generation for EMF validation for the given cell, as specified in 5G_L2_18398_replaced([11174436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26j42fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

### 2.2.5.9 Resource distribution to non GBR bearers of initial transmission UEs (ID: 11150106)

**2.2.5.9.0-1**  (ID: `11150114`)

Resource distribution to non GBR bearers of initial transmission UEs L2-PS shall distribute the available resources calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_4500_replaced([11179300](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4oDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to each initial transmission UE with non-GBR data belonging to drbTraffic which includes bearers with normal non-GBR and bearers with NBR excessive data(infers to bearer whose NBR is met in slot with dedicated resource allocation in earlier step in FD but still has data in buffer). CP2 Reference : 5G_UP_ALG_22858_replaced([11179788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku7ES_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For NBR bearers the scheduling weight to be used in this step will be the same as scheduling weight if this bearer would have been treated as normal non GBR bearer(example due to admission control)

---

##### 2.2.5.13.1.0-4 Aggregating Throughput for the Scheduled UE Special Handling in case of blocking due to Throughput Limit: (ID: 11150274)

**2.2.5.13.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11150278`)

Aggregating Throughput for the Scheduled UE NewTx:

- If a NewTx is dropped due to TP limit exceed:
- Release the HARQ Process
- The NDI bit shall remain same as prior to the dropped NewTx. In the next successful transmission the NDI needs to be toggled.

 ReTx:

- If a ReTx HARQ process is dropped due to TP limit exceed:
- It shall be put for ReTx scheduling.
- Consider this a not attempted ReTx i.e.: retain the value of rvIndexCounter, numTx, numAttemptsReTx. Increment numSkippedReTx.

 Note: These are just an indicative parameter list which have to be retained or updated.

---

#### 2.2.5.13.2 Throughput Pooling Interaction with Overload Control (ID: 11150285)
##### 2.2.5.13.2.0-1 Throughput Pooling Interaction with Overload Control Description: (ID: 11150292)

**2.2.5.13.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150296`)

Throughput Pooling Interaction with Overload Control if (tddInstTputPoolingAllowed == true) and if there is FD Overload:
 Skip the procedure described in 5G_L2_21247_replaced([11150243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24bK0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

do not update the counter BLOCKED_PDSCH_UE_COUNT (5G_L2_21251_replaced([11193049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28o8cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the UEs which are not processed due to overload.

end if

if (tddInstTputPoolingAllowed == true) and (if there NewTx is dropped due to throughput limit) and (if there is FD Overload)

Skip the procedure described in 5G_L2_21247_replaced([11150243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24bK0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Update the counter BLOCKED_PDSCH_UE_COUNT (5G_L2_21251_replaced([11193049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28o8cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the UEs which are not processed due to overload.

end if

## 2.2.6 DL PDCCH Scheduling (ID: 11150303)

**2.2.6.0-1**  (ID: `11150309`)

DL PDCCH Scheduling FA: [Internal Domain] PDCCH

Document Owner: Patrick Moisy (Nokia)

---

### 2.2.6.1 Creating and Sending DL DCI (ID: 11150315)
#### 2.2.6.1.1 DCI Format 1_1 (ID: 11150321)
##### 2.2.6.1.1.0-1 DCI Format 1_1 Bandwidth part indicator bits (ID: 11150326)

**2.2.6.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150334`)

DCI Format 1_1 If UE is configured with more than one dedicated BWP (including power saving BWP), L2PS shall use 2 bits for bandwidth part indicator field. See DCI 1_1 definition in 5G_UP_ALG_4443_replaced([11178081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku0Wk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Setting bandwidth part indicator field`s value, L2PS shall use bwpIndicator value for currently active BWP. See bwpIndicator definition in 5G_L2_149_replaced([11144092](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_233xOvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.2.6.1.2 CCEs resources (ID: 11150342)
##### 2.2.6.1.2.0-1 CCEs resources Number of Usable CCEs (ID: 11150347)

**2.2.6.1.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12824469`)

CCEs resources The number of usable CCEs in DL and UL direction is calculated based on the largest RB size coreset in pdcch configuration according to 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**or****according to 5G_UP_ALG_17155_replaced([11169994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt7lw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with dynamic PDCCH [CB007372-AA] and actAsymmetricDss = false **[End CB007372-AA]****

- Usable CCEs are calculated by DL and UL schedulers and use that according to the zone (upper or lower side of split) allocated to them for each search space, pdcch occasion and slot.

- If coreset is not split for a search space at a particuar pdcch occasion in a slot then non split CCEs will be used. Non split CCEs are either limited by BBRM DL alllocation or by coreset size.

In case of DSS enabled cell [CB007372-AA] with actAsymmetricDss = false **[End CB007372-AA], the algorithm proposed in 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is still applied based on following parameters**

- Max Aggregation level

- Min Aggregation level

- Coreset RB size

- DL CCE area of coreset

As only one coreset is used in a slot, the number of usable CCEs of that coreset will be considered and not the largest RB size coreset.

---

##### 2.2.6.1.2.0-2 CCEs resources CCEs assignment in case of 2 PMOs for PO for slot with UL and DL. (ID: 11150365)

**2.2.6.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11150371`)

CCEs resources Requirement is valid when actPagingSsbOptimization is equal to twoBeamsPerSlot.

In case of 2 PMOs in slot which requires CCEs for DL and UL direction assignment of CCEs for DL and UL Schedulers shall follow 5G_UP_ALG_29416_replaced([11169895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). CCEs distribution in this case shall be performed during slot pattern generation see 5G_UP_ALG_3970_replaced([11168960](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For number of usable CCEs see 5G_L2_4521_replaced([11150347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24bx4_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

This assignment can have place only when coreset used for paging scheduling has duration of 1 symbol and coreset size is equal to or bigger than 48 REGs. Ensured by PDL rule.

Setting twoBeamsPerSlot requires TDD and FR1 configuration.

For actPagingSsbOptimization see 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (PsCell_CellSetupReq).

---

#### 2.2.6.1.3 Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq (ID: 11150377)
##### 2.2.6.1.3.0-1 Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq Enabling/Disabling the transmission of DlData_PdcchSendReq to L1-DL (ID: 11150383)

**2.2.6.1.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150387`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq When rdEnablePdcchGrants = 0:

- The transmission of DlData_PdcchSendReq to L1-DL is disabled;

 When rdEnablePdcchGrants = 1 (default):

- The transmission of DlData_PdcchSendReq to L1-DL is enabled;

 Note: The sending of SmDataUe_PdcchInd to Airphone is enabled when a valid Airphone address is configured on L2-PS via PsTest_SubCellGroupInfoReq.

---

##### 2.2.6.1.3.0-2 Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq DL and UL PDCCH DCI applying to separate streams (ID: 11150395)

**2.2.6.1.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150406`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq If actDlSrsSubbandBm(ref 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 'true', DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be set to '5G_L2_494_replaced([11156008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248vSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))' except for the following IEs:

[CB009527-A] In eCPRI 7-2a (5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), [End CB009527-A]

DL and UL PDCCH DCIs are allocated in separate ceAxc to save beams per stream.

IE numCeAxCIndex set to 2

if DL DCI:

IE ceAxc set to {0, 1}

IE pdcchPrecodingOption4x4 set to repetitionOneXPol

if UL DCI:

IE ceAxc set to {2, 3}

IE pdcchPrecodingOption4x4 set to repetition2ndXPol

[CB009527-A] { In eCPRI 7-2e(5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , There is no limitation on number of beams per slot or per symbol in RU side, then there is no need for triggering DCI split for the purpose of saving beams per stream , refer 5G_UP_ALG_22202_replaced([11156841](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks311vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) . And there is no restriction that L1 supports such function, L2PS can keep the same algorithem like in eCPRI 7-2a, or disable by default }.[End CB009527-A]

---

#### 2.2.6.1.4 DCI fields setting (ID: 11150413)
##### 2.2.6.1.4.0-1 DCI fields setting DCI content (ID: 11150420)

**2.2.6.1.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150425`)

DCI fields setting The content of a DCI format 1_0 is described in 5G_UP_ALG_16216_replaced([11178050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuzvjPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The content of a DCI format 1_1 is described in 5G_UP_ALG_4443_replaced([11178081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku0Wk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note, please update the ttitrace event dlPdcchDciData defined in 5G_L2_12746_replaced([11205861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-IKNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if any DCI filed bit lenght changed.

---

##### 2.2.6.1.4.0-2 DCI fields setting counter DAI and total DAI calculation (ID: 11150432)

**2.2.6.1.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12763888`)

DCI fields setting To support ACK/NACK codebook type-2, 5G-L2-PS shall fill the correct C-DAI and T-DAI in DL DCI for each scheduled carrier (see 5G_UP_ALG_4466_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

During the FD scheduling for each subcell (carrier), when a UE is scheduled, the DlData_PdschSendReq and LoCtrl_PduMuxReq will be sent, but DlData_PdcchSendReq will not be sent at the same time.

5G-L2-PS will record all the scheduled UEs and the scheduled subcells during subcell level FD scheduling, at the same time L2-PS shall record the total number of subcells that are scheduled for each UE.

At every TTI, 5G-L2-PS shall update counter DAI, total DAI and fill DCI as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_4466_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Counter DAI is updated after the FD scheduling of all carriers. Total DAI is calculated in different phases depending on the configuration:

- For FR1, total DAI is updated in FD scheduling phase of each sub-cell

- For FR2, [Before CNI-137616-B]

o If rdEnablePucchPreallocation, defined in 5G_L2_4135_replaced([11181853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XKFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), is set to true, [End CNI-137616-B] total DAI is updated after the FD scheduling of all carriers [Before CNI-137616-B]

o If rdEnablePucchPreallocation, defined in 5G_L2_4135_replaced([11181853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XKFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Is set to false, total DAI is updated in FD scheduling phase of each cell [End CNI-137616-B]

For CA Ues using Distributed PUCCH algorithm(DPA) as described in 5G_L2_590_replaced([11158139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25JjnPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the counter DAI and total DAI shall not be calculated at or after FD scheduling phase. Instead, the counter DAI and total DAI used in the DCI is the one calculated by the DPA algorithm as described in 5G_L2_598_replaced([11158391](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KxvPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

CP2 reference(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_4466_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Downlink Assignment Index in DCI

5G_UP_ALG_15743_replaced([11204407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkqMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). area = {start PRB, number of PRB, start Symbol, numberOfSymbol} The area information for each of the resources (SR, HARQ, pCSI) will be sent by 5G-CP-RT to 5G-L2-PS during CellSetup request message (when the feature is enabled). 5G-L2-PS should send the region information(startPRB, numOfPRB, startSymbol, numOfSymbol) of the resources(SR,HARQ, pCSI) to L1 when an UE consumes any PRB in that region. (Ref: 5G_UP_ALG_15743_replaced([11204407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkqMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) In each of the areas, if a single PRB gets scheduled, whole area (SR and/or HARQ and/or pCSI) is indicated to L1, i.e.: **full PUCCH region are forwarded to L1, even if there is as little as 1 PRB each allocated for HARQ, SR, pCSI.** The regions are combined, and bigger region is formed if both regions have PRBs used by UE. **Ex: From the PUCCH allocation as given in below Picture - If UE1 has SR reception in PRB 2 and UE2 has HARQ reception at PRB 6, then complete SR and HARQ region are sent to L1 as one region i.e start PRB =1, number of PRB=12 {1,12} (as SR ={1,4}, HARQ={5,12})** If frequency hopping is enabled then the slot will be considered as 2 sub-slots and region defined for each of upper/lower, pre/post-frequency hop)

Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access).****Ex: Top half of PUCCH region****(SR area from 1 to 4PRB, HARQ 5 to 12, pCSI 13 to 24)******** PUCCH resource allocation (reservation) varies based on the number of Bandwidth parts. For all the cases 5G-CP-RT will share the static region information to 5G-L2-PS. Only in the cases where the [Before CB013152-A]feature CB006878 is enabled[CB013152-A]parameter actDynUlResAlloc is True, see [11142095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23sLDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)[End CB013152-A] – the shared static-region information of pCSI could vary based on scheduling decision. Hence when the feature is enabled the pCSI region information is to be picked dynamically every slot based on Scheduler allocation of pCSI to UE’s. Note: If actDynUlResAllocPhase2 is True[Before CB013152-A-UPD004] [CB013152-A]for FR1 TDD or actLongPucchResourceOpt is True for FR1 FDD cells[End CB013152-A][End CB013152-A-UPD004], then, based on the cell load, in the PUCCH area there is a dynamically added SRCX (SR Capacity eXtension) region, see [11204407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_s6wIIPvQEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11204436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_tC_eIPvQEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). Since 5G-CP-RT includes SRCX PRBs for computation of number of PRBs in the pCSI region, then 5G-L2-PS shall behave as when actDynUlResAlloc = True for handling pCSI area information. **IE Filling:** Every UlData_PucchReceiveReq 5G-L2-PS shall include the “pucchAreaBoundaries” in the message indicating the regions used. For achieving this, 5G-L2-PS will split the PUCCH areas into two ‘PUCCH Dedicated fragments’ (refer 5G_UP_ALG_15849_replaced([11204436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkqPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each of the configuration(single BWP, Multiple BWP, CB006878 enabled/disabled)). Each of the ‘dedicated fragments’ will be further split into 2 regions (0 to 6 Symbols, 7 to 13 Symbols) and the PUCCH area boundary will be shared with L1 based on PRB usage in that area. i.e there can be 4 pucchAreaBoundaries elements filled when both Top and Low PUCCH resources are used
Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access). PUCCH format 1 and 3 can be allocated in one PRB StartPRB and number of PRB’s in each of the “pucchAreaBoundaries” will be filled based on the region present within the Top and Bottom fragments (SR, HARQ, pCSI) (as required in 5G_UP_ALG_15849_replaced([11204436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkqPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) One example case with 100MHz BW, Single BWP config with 3 UE’s (RNTI’s) are shown below.
Could not load image (check sign-in and GCS access). 5G-L2-PS will align PucchAreaBoundaries-->eCpriConfig-->numCeAxCIndex and ceAxCIndex same as eCpriConfig under each RNTI. (PucchAreaBoundaries will be used for eCPRI enabled cases alone, so will be set to default value (reset) in other cases. Common PUCCH Boundary creation 5G-L2-PS will send the boundaries of the fragment (start and end PRB) that specifies the common PUCCH allocation. This includes both the upper and lower edge , before and after frequency hopping. However unlike dedicated PUCCH, this fragment will specify the PRBs that are actually scheduled in common PUCCH instead of sending the whole region for common PUCCH. But if there are empty PRB's identified in the Common PUCCH area (ex:case: 3 Upper and 3 Lower PRB Common PUCCH scenarios, Scenario 12 in xls below) sending absolute PRB will not be feasible with 5G_L1_IF_14907_replaced([11514064](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zLfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) interface. Hence 5G-L2-PS shall create common PUCCH area boundary considering the empty PRB into the area identified Such that the empty PRBs are not present in top and bottom of the area sent to L1. This approach is adapted to ensure that all the scheduled PRBs in Common PUCCH are included the PUCCH boundaries sent to L1 Possible combination of PUCCH area boundary examples with different configurations are captured in CB008941_PossibleBoundaryCombination_L1L2.xlsx

#### 2.2.7.1-1.0-2 PM Counter Support UlData_PucchReceiveReq (ID: 11150803)

**2.2.7.1-1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11150820`)

PM Counter Support 5G-L2-PS shall send a single UlData_PucchReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL of each subcell with at least one allocated PUCCH resource on a given slot for PUCCH reception.

For UE configured with Carrier Aggregation with at least one SCell PUCCH transmission is allocated only on PSCell (Joint-UCI), 5G-L2-PS shall send a UlData_PucchReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL of an PSCell to request the reception of PUCCH on that subcell.

If HARQ feedback is expected at a given slot, UlData_PucchReceiveReq message shall be sent to the corresponding subcell managing the PUCCH reception after DL scheduling of the last DL slot mapped to this slot and include any CSI or SR report reception which is expected in the same slot. Otherwise, message timing is relative to any CSI or SR report reception

For the timing requirement when UlData_PucchReceiveReq is expected to be received by 5G-L1-UL please refer to 5G_L1_5G21A_293 and 5G_L2_353_replaced([11151020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24gDUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For analog beamforming for eCPRI RUs, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the corresponding UE through ceAxcIndex and patternId in UlData_PucchReceiveReq according to 5G_L1_5G21A_215 as

ceAxcIndex eAxC index of default data for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_1516 and 5G_UP_ALG_5161_replaced([11204321](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

patternId map beam Id to pattern Id according to 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: Linked to both 5GC000399 and 5GC000918 features to avoid creating a dependency on their mutual implementation order. And based on CP3 discussion, 5GC000399-KX will fill ceAxcIndex and patternId.

In the Scell of FDD-TDD CA (FR1) [5GC001167-H]or FDD-FDD CA [End 5GC001167-H], L2-PS will not send UlData_PucchReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL after each PDSCH scheduling but send the scheduling result, including scheduling info[5GC001167-H](https://systeminsights.ext.net.nokia.com/not%20applicable%20to%20FDD-FDD%20CA)[End 5GC001167-H]for CA-UE and allocated PUCCH resource[5GC001167-H](https://systeminsights.ext.net.nokia.com/not%20applicable%20to%20FDD-FDD%20CA)[End 5GC001167-H] to P(S)Cell L2-PS.

Before sending UlData_PucchReceiveReq for any subcell, 5G-L2-PS shall judge whether certain subcell shall be buffered according to 5G_UP_ALG_5214_replaced([11209976](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). bufferedUlConfig is a structure used in UlData_PucchReceiveReq to control buffered UL usage and it shall be filled regardless of whether buffered UL is used or not (5G_L1_5G21A_264).

CP2 reference:

5G_UP_ALG_4602_replaced([11187378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PUCCH Reception request with Long PUCCH

---

#### 2.2.7.1.1 Requesting PUCCH reception (ID: 11150467)
##### 2.2.7.1.1.0-1 Requesting PUCCH reception Transmission timing of UlData_PucchReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL (ID: 11150472)

**2.2.7.1.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11150490`)

Requesting PUCCH reception In the implementation, PUCCH Reception Request is sent after the FD scheduling for each subcell because for carrier aggregation UE, the total number of ACK/NACK bit is needed. The PUCCH Reception Request sending is put together with PDCCH sending as 5G_L2_278_replaced([11150432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24cY8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Further timing aspects concerning Long PUCCH are given in 5G_L2_9898_replaced([11150497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24cY_PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

UlData_PucchReceiveReq for the UEs with Harq-Ack timing N+K1aCsi (see 5G_UP_ALG_4331_replaced([11177668](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be delayed until the slot N’ corresponding to the latest DL scheduler occasion with regular k1 timing (i.e. that slot N’ for which N + k1aCsi = N’ +k1), is completed. [CB009510-A-UPD001] Precalculated K1 timing can be redundant and may not coincide with the fact that the slot is schedulable (for that actual K1 timings, set at the very moment needs to be checked). [End CB009510-A-UPD001] The transmitted UlData_PucchReceiveReq shall be unified with the PUCCH reception requests corresponding available in last DL scheduling N’ for non A-CSI UEs.

---

##### 2.2.7.1.1.0-2 Requesting PUCCH reception Instance handling UlData_PucchReceiveReq (ID: 11150497)

**2.2.7.1.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150507`)

Requesting PUCCH reception In FDD [CB006064-A] and TDD FR1 [End CB006064-A], with long PUCCH configured, k1 > k2 > 1 (5G_UP_ALG_2473_replaced([11116092](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2484_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Hence DL and UL scheduler have at least ca. 2 slots time to synchronize wrt. requesting PUCCH or PUSCH reception from L1, based on the time duration between end of UL scheduling and end of corresponding L1 PUCCH/PUSCH receive windows (see also 5G_L1_5G21A_280). It is up to implementation to decide whether the UlData_PucchReceiveReq message handling shall be kept in DL Scheduler or moved to UL Scheduler, both should be possible with the time budget.

---

#### 2.2.7.1.2 PUCCH reception handling (ID: 11150514)
##### 2.2.7.1.2.0-1 PUCCH reception handling Reception of UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD or UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD (ID: 11150521)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11150531`)

PUCCH reception handling Upon reception of UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD or UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD, 5G-L2-PS shall perform:

- DL HARQ Handling (5G_UP_ALG_12737_replaced([11184145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),
- R&D Counter Handling for ACK/NACK bits on PUSCH as described in 5G_L2_302_replaced([11150602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dAD_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
- [CB009189-B] Counter handling as described in 5G_L2_8084_replaced([11150707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8086_replaced([11150721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8099_replaced([11150731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_8101_replaced([11150745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB009189-B].

 Notes:

- The ACK/NACK bits of ackNack IE are representing ACK/NACK of TB sent via each scheduled Cell in the UE according to counter DAI and total DAI in the DCI. In implementation, the mapping between bit and SCell info can be obtained from the bookkeeping table in 5G-L2-PS which is described in 5G_UP_ALG_4592_replaced([11187305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.2.7.1.2.0-2 PUCCH reception handling Reception of xPUCCH Information from 5G-L1-UL (ID: 11150538)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13362778`)

PUCCH reception handling For each UlData_PucchReceiveReq, 5G-L2-PS shall receive xPUCCH information from 5G-L1-UL via the messages UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD[CNI-136896-A], see [11514174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ),[End CNI-136896-A] and UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs[CNI-136896-A], see [11514246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BUPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)[End CNI-136896-A].

For each UlData_PuschReceiveReq requesting reception of UCI multiplexed in PUSCH, L2-PS shall receive UCI information from 5G-L1-UL via the message UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD.

---

##### 2.2.7.1.2.0-3 PUCCH reception handling Decoding of F1 SR overlapping with F3 HARQ for UEs configured with power saving BWP (ID: 11150549)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11150554`)

PUCCH reception handling This requirement applies only when actPowerSavingBwp is set to TRUE in the cell (5G_L2_IF_95_replaced([10968336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UXk5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When the UE has and both PUCCH F1 (for SR) and F3 (for HARQ feedback reporting) resources configured, L2-PS shall:

1) On SR occasion in slot with allocated F3 PUCCH resources for DL HARQ, request PUCCH reception from L1 for both resources (see 5G_L2_947_replaced([11180342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MK8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_954_replaced([11180444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MyA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), respectively).

Note: if SR is expected to be multiplexed in PUCCH F3 due to periodic CSI report, F1 request shall be skipped.

In case PUCCH response is received from L1 for both of these PUCCH resources, L2-PS shall:

1) Determine for both above-mentioned PUCCH formats, if positive SR can be detected there (from F1 – directly, from F3 – where SR can be multiplexed with HARQ feedback).

2) If positive SR can be found in any of these PUCCH resources, proceed with SR handling.

SFS reference and rationale: 5G_UP_ALG_31796_replaced([11187407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

See also 5G_UP_ALG_29170_replaced([11111382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpM2zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rdActPuschDtxOnSrSlotForBwpScanning, R&D parameter that enables capability to consider a Dtx PUSCH on SR slot as a Dtx PUSCH triggered by an UL grant due a positive SR.

---

##### 2.2.7.1.2.0-4 PUCCH reception handling Routing of the PUCCH Response Messages to L2-PS (ID: 11150561)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11150567`)

PUCCH reception handling UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD and UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs addresses in UlData_PucchReceiveReq shall be configured such that both responses are directed to the DL Scheduler.

[5GC000885-A] If UCI is expected to be multiplexed in PUSCH then UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD address of UlData_PuschReceiveReq shall be configured such that L1 sends UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD to the DL Scheduler. [end 5GC000885-A]

#### 2.2.7.1.3 PM Counter Support (ID: 11150573)
##### 2.2.7.1.3.0-1 PM Counter Support Scheduling Request (SR) on PUCCH format 1 R&D Counter Support for successful reception (nonDTX case) (ID: 11150577)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150583`)

PM Counter Support In case of pucch format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220), that carried a successful received positive SR as described in 5G_UP_ALG_4615_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) the below specified R&D counters shall be incremented.

[5GC000885-E] 5G_UP_ALG_4615_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) describes how to distinguish successful and unsuccessful receptions of PUCCH format 1 if one or two DL HARQ A/N are expected in same slot as SR. [end 5GC000885-E].

For each grant with successfully received positive SR the cell related R&D counter

M55303CRD58001, aka SUCC_SR_PUCCH_FORMAT1, shall be incremented. It describes the number of positive Scheduling Request (SR) indications that are successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) via message using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220).

SUCC_SR_PUCCH_FORMAT1 = SUCC_SR_PUCCH_FORMAT1 + 1

Note: The R&D counter for SR reception via Pucch format 3 is described in 5G_L2_300_replaced([11150590](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dADfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

CP2 requirement(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

##### 2.2.7.1.3.0-2 PM Counter Support Scheduling Request (SR) & Periodic CSI on PUCCH format 3 R&D Counter Support for successful reception (nonDTX case) (ID: 11150590)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11150596`)

PM Counter Support Upon reception of ulData_pucchReceiveRespPs message including grants of pucch format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220), that carry a successful received positive SR multiplexed with periodic CSI report below specified R&D counters shall be incremented.

For each grant including a successfully received positive SR the cell related R&D counter

M55303CRD59001, aka SUCC_SR_PUCCH_FORMAT3, describe the number of Scheduling Request indications that are successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) via using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220) shall be increased.

SUCC_SR_PUCCH_FORMAT3 = SUCC_SR_PUCCH_FORMAT3 + 1

Note: The R&D counter for SR reception via Pucch format 1 is described in 5G_L2_298_replaced([11150577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dAC_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each grant including a successfully received periodic CSI report the cell related R&D counter

M55303CRD60001, aka SUCC_PCSI_PUCCH_FORMAT3, describe the number of periodic CSI report indications that are successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220).

SUCC_PCSI_PUCCH_FORMAT3 = SUCC_PCSI_PUCCH_FORMAT3 + 1

These counters are an R&D counter.

CP2 requirement(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS
