##### 2.2.7.1.3.0-3 PM Counter Support HARQ A/N on PUSCH R&D Counter Support (ID: 11150602)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11150606`)

PM Counter Support Upon reception of ulData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD message (see 5G_L1_5G21A_209) L2-PS shall evaluate for each grant inside the meassage the structure ackOnPuschReportAndDtxMeas (see 5G_L1_5G21A_210) regarding whether it was received correctly, contains ACK/NACK and increase respective R&D counter.

[CB006064-A]

Depending of the number of ACK/NACK bits N received in ackOnPuschReportAndDtxMeas structure the following processing shall be performed:

In the case that N=1 A/N bit is expected the values for 1 A/N bit feedback (dtxAck1bit and ackNack1bitUci) shall be evaluated:

[End CB006064-A]

If (dtxAck1bit == nonDtx) {

M55303CRD62001 = M55303CR62001 + 1 , aka PUSCH_UCI_NON_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could be received due to nonDTX on UCI.

if (ackNack1bitUci = ack) {

M55303CRD56001 = M55303CRD56001 + 1 , aka HARQ_ACK_PUSCH_BIN1. This (histogram) R&D counter shall provide the number of successfully received HARQ A/N indications containing 'ACK' via PUSCH, when A/N there is only 1 ACK/NACK bits on PUSCH.

}

else if (ackNack1bitUci == nack) {

M55303CRD57001 = M55303CRD57001 + 1 , aka HARQ_NACK_PUSCH_BIN1. This (histogram) R&D counter shall provide the number of received HARQ A/N containing 'NACK' indications via PUSCH, when A/N there is only 1 ACK/NACK bits on PUSCH.

}

else if (dtxAck1bit == Dtx) {

M55303CRD61001 = M55303CRD61001 + 1 , aka PUSCH_UCI_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could not be received due to DTX on UCI.}

}

[CB006064-A]

In the case that N>=2 A/N bits feedback are expected the values for more than 1 A/N bit feedback (dtxAckMoreThan1Bit and ackNackUciMoreThan1Bit) shall be evaluated:

If (dtxAckMorethan1Bit == nonDtx) {

M55303CRD62001 = M55303CR62001 + 1 , aka PUSCH_UCI_NON_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could be received due to nonDTX on UCI.

for (n=0, n<N, ++n) {

if (ackNackUciMoreThan1Bit[n] == ack) ++ACKS

else if (ackNackUciMoreThan1Bit[n] == nack) ++NACKS

}

M55303CRD5600 = M55303CRD5600 + 1, aka HARQ_ACK_PUSCH_BIN. This (histogram) R&D counter shall provide the number of successfully received HARQ A/N indications containing ACKS 'ACK' via PUSCH.

M55303CRD5700 = M55303CRD5700 + 1, aka HARQ_NACK_PUSCH_BIN. This (histogram) R&D counter shall provide the number of received HARQ A/N containing NACKS 'NACK' indications via PUSCH.

ACKS=0; NACKS=0;

}

else if (dtxAckMoreThan1bit == Dtx) {

M55303CRD61001 = M55303CRD61001 + 1 , aka PUSCH_UCI_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could not be received due to DTX on UCI.}

}

[end CB006064-A]

Note: For 885-A (FDD) there is only 1 ACK/NACK bit included. For later subfeatures the single R&D counters become histogram counter with 8 bins.

[5GC000885-E] Note: For 885-E the PM Counters were extended by CSI reports according to 5G_L2_304_replaced([11150612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dnEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

CP2 requirement(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

##### 2.2.7.1.3.0-4 PM Counter Support CSI on PUSCH R&D Counter Support (ID: 11150612)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11150619`)

PM Counter Support Upon reception of ulData_PuschReceiveRespPs message (see 5G_L1_5G21A_199) L2-PS shall evaluate for each report inside the meassage the structure csiOnPuschDtxMeas (see 5G_L1_5G21A_202) regarding whether it was received correctly and increase respective R&D counter.

If (dtxCsiPart1 == nonDtx) {

M55303CRD62001 = M55303CR62001 + 1 , aka PUSCH_UCI_NON_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

reports that could be received correctly due to nonDTX on UCI.

}

else if (dtxCsiPart1 == Dtx) {

M55303CRD61001 = M55303CRD61001 + 1 , aka PUSCH_UCI_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

reports that could not be received correctly due to DTX on UCI.}

}

Note: For 885-A the HARQ A/N on PUSCH was implemented for this PM Counters (see 5G_UP_1496_replaced([11359646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucpBlPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

CP2 requirement(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

##### 2.2.7.1.3.0-5 PM Counter Support HARQ A/N on PUCCH R&D Counter Support for successful reception (nonDTX case) (ID: 11150627)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11150635`)

PM Counter Support "UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message (5G_L1_5G21A_223) is received by L2-PS from UL-L1 cell related R&D Counters on UL UCI on PUCCH of class 'NR UL Signal Quality Level' shall be handled. For each grant/pucch allocation the 'dtx' field in the 'pucchDtxMeasurement' struct shall be evaluatied and for sucessful reception (dtx=nonDTX) the following R&D counters shall be processed.

The R&D counter are only used in cell configuration with long PUCCH. So depending on the Pucch format field ('pucchFormat' 1 or 3) of each pucch allocation two cases shal be distinguished:

Case 1: HARQ A/N on PUCCH format 1 successful detection

In case of pucch format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220) the following cell related R&D counters shall be incremented:

[5GC000885-E] 5G_UP_ALG_4615_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) describes how to distinguish successful and unsuccessful receptions of PUCCH format 1 if one or two DL HARQ A/N are expected in same slot as SR. [end 5GC000885-E].

The HARQ A/N R&D Counters for pucch format 1 shall be done the following steps:

1.) The number of HARQ bits nANPucch ( see 5G_L1_5G21A_218) in corresponding uldata_pucchReceiveReq message shall be assessed and in the array 'ackNack' (with up to 8 elements) of the pucch allocation insdie UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD shall be evaluated. The number of ack ( =1 ) - bits called = 'numOfAcks' and nack (=0) bits called 'numOfNacks' inside the ackNack array are counted.

2.)Depending on 'numOfAcks' ( 0.. 2 ):

M55303CRD52001 … M55303CRD52002 aka HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN1 … HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN2 dscribe the histogram for the number of 'acked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) message using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220)

Switch ( numOfAcks) {

Case 1: HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN1 = HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN2 = HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT2_BIN1 + 1;

}

3.)Depending on 'numOfNacks' ( 0.. 2 ):

M55303CRD53001 … M55303CRD53002 aka HARQ_NACK_AN_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN1 … HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN2 dscribe the histogram for the number of 'nacked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) message using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220)

Switch ( numOfNacks) {

Case 1: HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN1 = HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN2 = HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT1_BIN2 + 1;

}

Case 2: HARQ A/N on PUCCH format 3 successful detection

In case of pucch format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220) the follwoing cell related R&D counters shall be incremented:

The HARQ A/N R&D Counters for pucch format 3 shall be handled with the following steps:

1.) The number of HARQ bits nANPucch ( see 5G_L1_5G21A_218) in correspnding uldata_pucchReceiveReq message shall be assessed and in the array 'ackNack' (with up to 8 elements) of the pucch allocation insdie UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD shall be evaluated. The number of ack ( =1 ) - bits called = 'numOfAcks' and nack (=0) bits called 'numOfNacks' inside the ackNack array are counted.

2.)Depending on 'numOfAcks' ( 0.. 8 ):

M55303CRD54001 … M55303CRD42008 aka HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN1 … HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN8 dscribe the histogram for the number of 'acked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) message using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220).

Switch ( numOfAcks) {

Case 1: HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN1 = HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN2 = HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN2 + 1;

...

Case 8: HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN8 = HARQ_ACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN8 + 1;

}

3.) Depending on 'numOfNacks' ( 0.. 8 ):

M55303CRD55001 … M55303CRD55008 aka HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN1 … HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN8 dscribe the histogram for the number of 'nacked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) message using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220)

Switch ( numOfNacks) {

Case 1: HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN1 = HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN2 = HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN2 + 1;

...

Case 8: HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN8 = HARQ_NACK_PUCCH_FORMAT3_BIN8 + 1;

}

CP2 requirement(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

##### 2.2.7.1.3.0-6 PM Counter Support UL PUCCH OFDM Symbol Usage PM Counter Support (ID: 11150642)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11150648`)

PM Counter Support Upon sending of a "UlData_PucchReceiveReq message (according to 5G_L1_5G21A_215) by L2-PS to UL-L1 PM Counters of class 'NR Cell Utilitzation' related to used PUCCH OFDM symbols shall be incremented for the related subcell.

M55308C03004, aka PUCCH_OFDM_SYMBOLS, indicates the accumulated number (sum) of OFDM symbols used for PUCCH in the related subcell.

The UlData_PucchReceiveReq message (5G_L1_5G21A_215) shall contain a list of PUCCH resources per subcell that shall be used by 5G-L2-PS to trigger 5G-L1-UL to decode the NR UL slot. These UL resources shall be evaluated one-by-one:

1.) First the number of subcells in the message shall be determined

2.) For each subcell the related cell shall be identified via subcellID mapping and shall be stored.

3.) Then the number of PUCCH resources inside the subcell shall be identifed via parameter 'numOfPucchResources'

4.) Loop through the UL PUCCH resources by evaluation the parameters.

5.) With parameter 'firstSymbol and numOfPucchSymbols' the number of OFDM PUCCH symbols shall be assessed

6.) For the related cell's PM counter shall be incremented:

PUCCH_OFDM_SYMBOLS = PUCCH_OFDM_SYMBOLS + 'numOfPucchSymbols'

Note: Above process description is general considering multiple subcells per message and multiple PUCCH resources per subcell. Starting with 1 subcell per cell and 1 PUCCH resource per subcell these numbers will be increased step-by-step by later features.

CP2 requirement(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

##### 2.2.7.1.3.0-7 PM Counter Support UL PUCCH Quality PM Counters for successful (nonDTX) reception case (ID: 11150654)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11150668`)

PM Counter Support When a valid (dtx=nonDTX) "UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs message (5G_L1_5G21A_220) is received by L2-PS from UL-L1 PM Counters of class 'NR UL Signal Quality Level' shall be handled. 5G_UP_ALG_4615_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) describes how to distinguish successful and unsuccessful receptions of PUCCH format 1 if one or two DL HARQ A/N are expected in same slot as SR.

These PM counter statistics describe the distribution UL PUCCH Quality values by 6, 18- or 44 bin-histograms.

These PM counter(s) are defined per subcell and every UE's nonDTX UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs messages in this subcell are contributing to these counters.

The following PM counters / counter bins shall be incremented +1 in the non-DTX case.

1.) PUCCH format 0 successful detection

M55303C12001, aka PUCCH_FORMAT0_NON_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 0 ('pucchFormat' == 0 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220).

2.) PUCCH format 2 successful detection

M55303C16001, aka PUCCH_FORMAT2_NON_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 2 ('pucchFormat' == 2 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220).

3.) UL RSSI on PUCCH Histogram

M55303C09001… M55303C09044, aka UE_RSSI_PUCCH_LEVEL_01 ... UE_RSSI_PUCCH_LEVEL_44, are describing the received UE related RSSI for PUCCH Level xx. It is the UE related Received Signal Strenth Indicator (RSSI) distribution for PUCCH containing also interference and noise. Measurement is calculated over all PRBs allocated for a UE and normalized to a single PRB. It is measured in the gNB and provided by UL-L1 in the parameter field 'rssi' (see 5G_L1_5G21A_220). The value is received in the unit dBm.

The UL PUCCH RSSI histogram consists of 44 bins with 2dBm-width:

UE_RSSI_PUCCH_LEVEL_01: [rssi <= -114dBm]

UE_RSSI_PUCCH_LEVEL_02: [-114dBm < rssi <= -112dBm]

UE_RSSI_PUCCH_LEVEL_03: [-112dBm < rssi <= -110dBm]

…

UE_RSSI_PUCCH_LEVEL_44: [-30dBm < rssi]

Value -140dBm shall be considered as invalid and counter shall NOT be updated.

4.) UL SINR on PUCCH Histogram

M55303C08001… M55303C08018, aka UE_SINR_PUCCH_LEVEL_01 ... UE_SINR_PUCCH_LEVEL_18, are describing the received UE related SINR for PUCCH Level xx. It is the UE related Signal to Interference and Noise Ratio (SINR) distribution for PUCCH, measured in the gNB and provided by UL-L1 in the parameter field 'sinr' ( see 5G_L1_5G21A_220). The value is received in the unit dB.

The UL PUCCH SINR histogram consists of 18 bins with 2dB-width:

UE_SINR_PUCCH_LEVEL_01: [sinr <= -8dB]

UE_SINR_PUCCH_LEVEL_02: [-8dB < sinr <= -6dB]

UE_SINR_PUCCH_LEVEL_03: [-6dB < sinr <= -4dB]

…

UE_SINR_PUCCH_LEVEL_18: [24dB < sinr]

Only 1 layer transmission is supported. NO SINR averaging over two layers is not done.

When two separate SINR values for the two layers are received, dB-average shall be calculated and counter shall be updated only once. Introduced by multi-layer feature.

5.) PUCCH format 1 successful detection

M55303C14001, aka PUCCH_FORMAT1_NON_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220). L2-PS shall not count/consider PUCCHs reporting SR only.

6.) PUCCH format 3 successful detection

M55303C18001, aka PUCCH_FORMAT3_NON_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G_L1_5G21A_220).

[CB007103-B] 7.) PUCCH format 3 successful detection with Rel.16 DMRS

Refer to 5G_L2_16103_replaced([11193174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28pjivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB007103-B]

CP2 requirement(s):

- 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

### 2.2.8.2 Post TD scheduler (ID: 11150856)
#### 2.2.8.2.0-1 Post TD scheduler Determine the number of UEs sharing given PRB (ID: 11150861)

**2.2.8.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11150877`)

Post TD scheduler If basic MU-MIMO is activated for a cell (actDlMuMimo is set to true & actDlMuMimoEnh is set to false (ref. 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_109_replaced([10968696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UZaEfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_1871_replaced([10968710](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UZaE_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), a specialized PRB bookkeeping method needs to be applied (ref. 5G_UP_ALG_8352_replaced([11191477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvhhOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In order to calculate PRB bookkeeping factors (rrmPrbBkFactor) and number of unallocated PRBs (rrmInstPrbFree) in Pair Size based PRB Bookkeeping (ref. 5G_UP_ALG_8156_replaced([11191504](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvhhPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) distribution of UEs between PRBs must be known.

L2-PS shall convert rat0Bitmap (ref. [Before CNI-116869-D] 5G_L2_321_replaced([11149724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24XgfvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[CNI-116869-D] 5G_L2_887_replaced([11178401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CNI-116869-D]) to prbAllocation for all scheduled UEs within a given cell and then sum up prbAllocation for all scheduled UEs to determine the number of UEs sharing given PRB:

prbAllocation for UE1: [x1_0, x1_1, ..., x1_lastIdx]

prbAllocation for UE2: [x2_0, x2_1, ..., x2_lastIdx]

...

sum of prbAllocation for all scheduled UEs:

ueSumInEachPrb = [x1_0 + x2_0 + ..., x1_1 + x2_1 + ..., ..., x1_lastIdx + x2_lastIdx + ...]

where:

x = 0 | 1

lastIdx <= 272

Calculated array determines how many UEs share given PRB within a given cell.

Number of UEs sharing given PRB equal to 0 means that this PRB is unallocated (free).

Number of unallocated PRBs (rrmInstPrbFree) equal to number of zeros in ueSumInEachPrb.

---

#### 2.2.8.2.0-2 Post TD scheduler Create Best NK list (ID: 12736750)

**2.2.8.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12736765`)

Post TD scheduler select UEs from CS1 list at current slot to create Best NK list, the algorithm see [12517582: Prepare best N and K list](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_U2PXwBiDEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Note:

BestNKListSize = Ceil (BestNKListRatio * [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A] cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A]);

K UEs = Ceil (BestNKListSize * BestKRatio);

N UEs = BestNKListSize - K UEs;

where

BestNKListRatio:NRBTS/NRCELL/dlBestNListRatio.

[Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size:avgCs1Size of next scheduling slot type(DL or BI slottype), see [11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
 [CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive: cs1ListMaxSizePreventive of next scheduling slot type(DL or BI slottype), see [11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CNI-136895-A])

BestKRatio:rdDlHighBuffBestKRatio (see [12532524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_bfiC4BuXEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

L2-PS shall calculate BLER for mute slots based on the PDSCH real transmitions, the algorithm see [12709975: BLER calculation for SSB slots](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_eBYD8mXaEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

L2-PS shall run the algorithm of the SSB interference Mitigation for non-BF as the bellow:

1. Upon reception of cell set up or reconfig, (for conditions [12709089: Basic functionality](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pAtj4GOsEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. Start/stop PRB muting and BLER calculation based on NRCELL.actSsbIMForNonBF, note: the start of BLER calculation shall be slot 0 after cell set up or reconfig.
3. Start/reset the r&d timer rdPeriodForSsbIM to start SSB slot BLER statistics
4. Store new SSB muted parameters

  1. If slotForSsbIM, blerThresForSsbIM shall be changed , PRB muting shall be stopped and reinitialized
  2. If cRbStartForSsbIM changes, the new value shall be applied in PRB muting

5. Initialize the BLER calculation
6. In the end of each 10 rdPeriodForSsbIM periods,
7. Run the BLER for SSB Slots algorithm, (for conditions refer to [12709975: BLER calculation for SSB slots](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_eBYD8mXaEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
8. Decide whether or not, (for conditions refer to [12709089: Basic functionality](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pAtj4GOsEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

  1. The specified PRBs shall be muted for the candidate DL slot([12707696: Configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8CsJcWLPEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
  2. The prohibit timer([12731408: rdProhibitTimerForSsbIM](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_p4zdEnNQEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) shall be started/restarted

9. During each of rdProhibitTimerForSsbIM (20 rdPeriodForSsbIM) in muted PRB of the slots defined by [12709089: Basic functionality](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pAtj4GOsEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
10. Not allocate the muted SSB PRB except common channel(SIB,Paging)
11. If there are timer out of the 10 rdPeriodForSsbIM periods for SSB muted slot BLER statistics during the prohibitTimer and BLER falls below the threshold, then muted PRBs shall still be muted and can not used

 Based on the above procedure of the algorithm and the configuration of rdProhibitTimerForSsbIM and default 10 rdPeriodForSsbIM periods for SSB interference mitigation, there are three case listed as the bellow( A,B,C.b is the step of the above algorithm of the SSB interference Mitigation. :

### 2.2.8.3 Optimized Flow Control (ID: 11150883)
#### 2.2.8.3.0-1 Optimized Flow Control Idle Timer Expiry (ID: 11150890)

**2.2.8.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12733843`)

Optimized Flow Control **[Before PR843369]
 On rdEthUpdateTimer expiry, L2-PS
 **[PR843369]
 When both of the following conditions are met:****

1. rdEthUpdateTimer has expired for the given UE
2. and the [12733172: Limit of maximum number of eTh updates for idle UEs in the given slot](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CyemUnRXEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) has not been reached,

 then 5G-L2-PS [End PR843369]**shall schedule eTh recalculation for associated Ue (see 5G_UP_ALG_4676_replaced([11192682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

This recalculation shall be performed in non real-time context to reduce impact on real-time scheduling performance. In high load scenario calculations may be postponed to next slots (as they are done in non real-time context). If eTh recalculations triggered in the previous two slots haven't finished, 5G-L2-PS shall postpone triggering new eTh recalculations to next slots.

If calculated eTh is sufficiently different from lastSentEth (see 5G_UP_ALG_15751_replaced([11192830](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvnn0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details), L2-PS shall:

- sent eTh to L2-LO using LoCtrl_DlUuStatusUpdateInd message (5G_L2_IF_4305_replaced([10985413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WH4Yfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
 Note: If the maximum number of bearers in message is exceeded L2_PS should send multiple messages. All bearers related to the single Ue should be sent within one message and should not be split between separate messages.
- store eTh in Ue context as lastSentEth to be used in next eTh update

---

#### 2.2.8.3.0-2 Optimized Flow Control Idle Timer Start/Restart (ID: 11150910)

**2.2.8.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150926`)

Optimized Flow Control L2-PS shall start a timer for each UE to trigger eTh calculation in absence of DL scheduling. The timer interval is [Before PR784119] specified by rdEthUpdateTimer (5G_UP_ALG_15747_replaced([11193522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvtucfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). On the timer expiry L2-PS shall re-start it, set interval to rdEthUpdateTimer and follow 5G_L2_10486_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

To prevent triggering overload control in high load scenarios, L2-PS during DL scheduling shall restart eTh update timer and set interval to: rdEthUpdateTimer + additional load adjusted interval. Additional interval value shall be calculated using data from overload control, ‘skippedUes’ to ‘numToBeScheduledUes’ ratio (5G_L2_1859_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_1675_replaced([11203797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and shall not exceed 100 ms.

For example:

If calculated ratio is 0 (no UEs are skipped), additional load adjusted interval shall be 0

If calculated ratio is 1 (all UEs are skipped), additional load adjusted interval shall be 100 ms

[PR784119] rdEthUpdateTimer (5G_UP_ALG_15747_replaced([11193522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvtucfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + load adjusted interval. On the timer expiry 5G-L2-PS shall restart the timer, set interval to rdEthUpdateTimer + load adjusted interval and follow 5G_L2_10486_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

To prevent triggering overload control or using too many resources in high load scenarios, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate load adjusted interval. This interval is calculated as follows:

(1) 5G-L2-PS shall monitor the completion status of previously triggered eTh calculations. It shall calculate the ratio of slots where new calculations were postponed due to ongoing previous calculations (see 5G_L2_10486_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the past 10 eTh calculation triggers. Based on this ratio, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate the load adjusted interval using the formula: ratio * 100 [ms].

For example:

If calculated ratio is 0 (none of the eTh recalculations were postponed), the load adjusted interval shall be 0 ms

If calculated ratio is 1 (all of the eTh recalculations in previous slots were postponed), the load adjusted interval shall be 100 ms

For FR2:

Interval shall be calculated by choosing max value calculated in (1) and value calculated using data from overload control, mean ‘skippedUes’ to ‘numToBeScheduledUes’ ratio from 5 slots (5G_L2_1859_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_1675_replaced([11203797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))using the formula: mean ratio * 100 [ms].

For example:

If calculated mean ratio is 0 (no UEs were skipped in 5 slots), the load adjusted interval shall be 0

If calculated mean ratio is 1 (all UEs were skipped in 5 slots), the load adjusted interval shall be 100 ms

[End PR784119]

---

#### 2.2.8.3.0-3 Optimized Flow Control Limit of maximum number of eTh updates for idle UEs in the given slot (ID: 12733172)

**2.2.8.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12733174`)

Optimized Flow Control When updating the estimated throughput for idle UEs, then 5G-L2-PS shall limit the number of updates in the given slot to the maximum value defined by one of the following parameters, based on the cell's frequencyRange (obtained from the [10966093: PsCnfg_AddressDistributionReq message content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UL-vvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) from the [0966124: L2RtPoolDeploymentInformations structure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)):

- If frequencyRange is FR2: [12733120: rdMaxNumOfIdleUeEthUpdatesPerFr2Slot](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LE-sMHRQEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
- Otherwise: [12733116: rdMaxNumOfIdleUeEthUpdatesPerFr1Slot](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_h-Au4HRPEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

### 2.2.8.4 Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature (ID: 11150931)
#### 2.2.8.4.0-1 Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature Achieved muting ratio calculation (ID: 11150937)

**2.2.8.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150942`)

Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature achievedMutingRatio computation is explained in 5G_UP_ALG_20824_replaced([11183727](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvMxFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Additional conditions to be applied at L2-PS are listed below

1. achievedMutingRatio must be computed in every DL/Special Slot (irrespective of the slot muting decision) as long as rfCoolingMode = true

2. When PsCell_SlotBlankingReq (with rfCoolingMode = True and with modified tgtMutingRatio) is received at L2-PS in slot n, the achievedMutingRatio shall be initialized / reset to the value of new tgtMutingRatio not later than in slot n+1.

3. When rfCoolingMode = False or when the feature is turned off, L2-PS internally maintains the value of tgtMutingRatio and achievedMuting Ratio as 1.00 (100%).

[PR720039]

1. In case of special slot, SlotmutingOutcomeNormalized shall be used instead of SlotmutingOutcome during the achievedMutingRatio computation.

 [End PR720039]

---

#### 2.2.8.4.0-2 Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature Slot muting outcome calculation (ID: 11150950)

**2.2.8.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150966`)

Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature SlotMutingOutcome computation is explained in 5G_UP_ALG_20825_replaced([11183747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvMxGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Additional conditions to be applied at L2-PS are listed below

1. SlotMutingOutcome must be computed in every DL/Special Slot (irrespective of the slot muting decision) as long as rfCoolingMode = true

2. SlotmutingOutcome[i] shall be initialized with value 0 when (i) rfCoolingMode = false OR (ii) In the first slot when rfCoolingMode = true

3. nSym_not_used [Before CB011114-B] shall comprise the total unused symbols after PDCCH + PDSCH + all other resource allocation [CB011114-B] is equal to nSym_total - total number of symbols used [End CB011114-B] on the DL/Special slot

4. nSym_not_used shall be computed/considered even when there are symbols left unused due to natural scheduling (DL/Special slots with 1 or more unused symbols)

5. SlotMutingOutcome shall be computed after computing achievedMutingRatio in a given DL/Special slot

6. SlotmutingOutcome for special slots shall be normalized based on total number of symbols for DL slot as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_20825_replaced([11183747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvMxGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The method to apply normalization shall be

SlotmutingOutcomeNormalized[i] = SlotmutingOutcome[i] x (nSym_total_spl(i) / nSym_total_dl(i))

with:

i index of DL/special slot

SlotmutingOutcome[i] SlotmutingOutcome before normalization computed as per 5G_UP_ALG_ 20825

SlotmutingOutcomeNormalized[i] SlotmutingOutcome after normalization

nSym_total_spl total DL symbols per special slot

nSym_total_dl total DL symbols per DL slot (non special slot). Refer 5G_UP_ALG_2313_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB011114-A]

1. For FDD, nSym_total is the total number of DL symbols per DL slot. It is equal to 14 OFDM Symbols.

 [End CB011114-A]

[CB011114-B]

If the FDD cell is shared with LTE, then nSym_total is the number of symbols applicable for NR DL transmissions. It is equal to 12 OFDM Symbols.

1. For a FDD Cell shared with LTE, symbols used for LTE CRS Rate Matching are considered as symbols applicable for NR DL transmissions.

 [End CB011114-B]

---

## 2.2.9 Slot Timing (ID: 11150971)

**2.2.9.0-1**  (ID: `11150976`)

Slot Timing Document Owner

Xie, Yuanying (NSB - CN/Hangzhou)

---

### 2.2.9.0-2 Slot Timing Slot Start (ID: 11150981)

**2.2.9.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `13382954`)

Slot Timing The DL Scheduler shall start the NR-slot-based processing at a time which guarantees that the L1-DL constraints wrt. the various message receive windows (described in 5G_L1_5G21A_121 ff.) are respected.

Based on those, the DL Scheduler processing for an NR-slot shall start x us before the NR-slot boundary at the gNB antenna

- following synchronization procedure described in 5G_L1L2_FLOW_671_replaced([11177460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTrwfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L1L2_FLOW_672_replaced([11177470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTrwvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 whereby x is set

- to (SlotOffsetDl + OneWayHwDelayDlc + AdditionalFddOffset), where

- AdditionalFddOffset is set to 750us if FDD cell is on Loki or Thor [CB014419-SR-EC] or Odin [End CB014419-SR-EC] based BB board, 30us if FDD cell is on ABIL based BB board, 0 otherwise.

- **FDD: *SlotOffsetDl = constant 1000us (1 slot) with SCS15kHz.***

- *SlotOffsetDl = constant 1000us (2 NR-slots) for below 6GHz configuration (SCS30kHz)*
- *SlotOffsetDl = constant 375us (3 NR-slots) for above 6GHz configuration (SCS120kHz)*
- *SlotOffsetDl can be overriden in testing with R&D parameter rdSlotOffsetAdjustmentDl by setting it to value other than 0xFFFFFFFF. Unit is microseconds.*
- *OneWayHwDelayDl = Value is read from PsCell_CellSetupReq if rd579LongFiberActivated is set to “1” and rdSlotTimerServiceEnabled is set to “1”. Otherwise it remains at initialization value of 50us.*
- **OneWayHwDelayDl = Value is always read from PsCell_CellSetupReq for All in Cloud product**
- *OneWayHwDelayDl can be overriden in testing with R&D parameter rdOverrideOneWayHwDelayDl (5G_L2_3476_replaced([11182008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) by setting it to value other than 0xFFFFFFFF. Unit is microseconds.*
- In case the configured *OneWayHwDelayDl is longer than slot duration then a correction is applied:*
- **SlotOffsetDl is extended by RoundDownToInt(OneWayHwDelayDl/SlotDuration) slots**
- *OneWayHwDelayDl is shortened to OneWayHwDelayDl mod SlotDuration microseconds*
- For example, if *OneWayHwDelayDl is (1.6 slots * slotduration) microseconds then the correction increases *SlotOffsetDl by one slot and *OneWayHwDelayDl becomes (0.6 slots * slotduration) microseconds.***
- When the actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is not set to "disabled" and the 750us timing pattern is activated (as described in 5G_L2_22818_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the SlotOffsetDl is extended by one slot. (refer to 750us timing pattern defined in 5G_UP_13436_replaced([11388805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufMmUfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
- When FR1 TDD frame structure is configured with tdLte Config0, the slotOffsetDl for each slot is not a fixed value any more, flexible slotOffsetDl value shall be used based on the table as described in 5G_L2_23169_replaced([11157417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25FSLvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 5GTimer is always used.

Note, also 5G_L2_353_replaced([11151020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24gDUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) depicts the affected messages and timings including L2-LO.

---

## 2.2.10 DL L1-L2 timing requirement (ID: 12710332)

**2.2.10.0-5**  (ID: `12712456`)

DL L1-L2 timing requirement Statistics of Late DL Messages Sent to L1:

L2-PS must maintain late DL data send messages sent to L1 and total DL data send messages sent to L1 over a period of second. These statistics are printed using VIP logs if there exists any late message during 1 second observation period. These counters are maintained for each message mentioned in [12710358: Time stamping of L2-PS DL messages to L1](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OG0cM2YQEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

## 2.2.11 DL Pipeline Scheduling (ID: 13442684)
### 2.2.11.1 Overview (informative) (ID: 13448743)
#### 2.2.11.1.0-1 Overview (informative) Concept (ID: 13448744)

**2.2.11.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448745`)

Overview (informative) Basic concepts with DL pipeline scheduling introduced.

DL TD EO: Includes DlPre Scheduler, DlTd Scheduler, DlPost Scheduler and DlNrt.

DL FD EO: Includes DlFdm Scheduler and DlFd Scheduler.

UL EO: Includes all UL Schedulers and UlNrt. No change with DL pipeline scheduling introduced.

DL Core: Where DL TD EO is running, DL FD EO will run on this core on non-pipeline slot(see [13448749: Slot Processing Type](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8thWsCiyEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

UL Core: Where UL EO isrunning, DL FD EO will run on this core on pipeline slot(see [13448749: Slot Processing Type](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8thWsCiyEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

---

#### 2.2.11.1.0-2 Overview (informative) Scheduling Type (ID: 13448747)
##### 2.2.11.1.0-2.0-1 Overview (informative) Sequential Scheduling (ID: 13451409)

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448748`)

Overview (informative) Sequential scheduling means that schedlers are run as planned order, Pre -> Td -> Fdm -> Fd -> Post.
 At the same time, when schedulers are running, Nrt messages can’t be handled.

---

##### 2.2.11.1.0-2.0-2 Overview (informative) Parallel Scheduling (ID: 13451419)

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13451420`)

Overview (informative) Parallel scheduling means that DlNrt and Dl FD EO can run on the two cores parallelly.
 But the critical path (DlPre, DlTd, DlFdm, DlFd, DlPost) still run sequentially as planned order.

This scheduling mode is introduced by CB012971-WB. will be obselete by CB014670?

---

##### 2.2.11.1.0-2.0-3 Overview (informative) Pipeline Scheduling (ID: 13451421)

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13451422`)

Overview (informative) Pipeline scheduling means that DL TD EO(DlPre, DlTd, DlPost and DlNrt) run on DL Core and DL FD EO(DlFdm and DlFd) run on UL Core parallelly.

Note:
 1. Because DlFdm/DlFd is triggered by DlTd, so DlPre/DlTd/DlPost and DlFdm/DlFd with the same xsfn are always run sequentially although they are run on two cores.
 2. For same component, the sequence shall be kept. e.g. DlPost(N) shall alwasy run ahead of DlPost(N+1).

---

#### 2.2.11.1.0-3 Overview (informative) Slot Processing Type (ID: 13448749)
##### 2.2.11.1.0-3.0-1 Overview (informative) Normal Pipeline Slot (ID: 13451411)

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448750`)

Overview (informative) Normal pipeline slot are slots which pipeline scheduling(see [13451421: Pipeline Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_zjhxoCmJEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is applied except the last one before UL scheduling slot.

Pipeline scheduling is applied when feature flag(will be define in CB014670-C) is enanbled and pipeline scheduling switched to ON(see [13448854: Dynamic Switch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlE4UCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), will be define in CB014670-C).

In normal pipeline slots, the DL TD EO and DL FO EO run concurrently on the DL Core and UL Core.

---

##### 2.2.11.1.0-3.0-2 Overview (informative) Last Pipeline Slot (ID: 13451415)

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13451416`)

Overview (informative) Last pipeline slot are the last slots before UL scheduling slot which pipeline scheduling(see [13451421: Pipeline Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_zjhxoCmJEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is applied.

Pipeline scheduling is applied when feature flag(will be define in CB014670-C) is enanbled and pipeline scheduling switched to ON(see [13448854: Dynamic Switch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlE4UCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), will be define in CB014670-C).

In last pipeline slots, the DL TD EO and DL FO EO run concurrently on the DL Core and UL Core.

---

##### 2.2.11.1.0-3.0-3 Overview (informative) Non-Pipeline Slot (ID: 13451412)

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13451413`)

Overview (informative) Non-pipeline slot are the slots sequential scheduling (see [13451409: Sequential Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ddxi0SmGEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is enabled.

In non-pipeline slots, both DL TD EO and DL FO EO run on DL Core.

---

#### 2.2.11.1.0-4 Overview (informative) Overall Example (ID: 13448751)

**2.2.11.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13448752`)

Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) 13448752: Overview (informative) This is an example to explain the basic scheduling process of pipeline enabled.

### 2.2.11.2 Cs2 Filter (ID: 13448754)
#### 2.2.11.2.0-1 Cs2 Filter Introduction (ID: 13448755)

**2.2.11.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448756`)

Cs2 Filter Since DL TD EO(DlPre, DlTd, DlPost and DlNrt) and DL FD EO(DlFdm and DlFd) can run on different cores parallelly which will introduce data race while the two EOs may visit the same UE context/DB.

To avoid the conflict, cs2Filter is introduced. cs2Filter is a UE list including the UEs selected by Pre/TD in Cs2List for current slot.

cs2Filter is maintained and used in DL TD EO to avoid data race with DL FD EO. The idea is that when UEs are scheduling on DL FD EO, these UEs shall not be visited/handled in DL TD EO at the same time.

---

#### 2.2.11.2.0-2 Cs2 Filter Housekeeping (ID: 13448764)
##### 2.2.11.2.0-2.0-1 Cs2 Filter Initialization (ID: 13452038)

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448765`)

Cs2 Filter Cs2Filter shall be set as empty at the startup, e.g. during cell setup.

---

##### 2.2.11.2.0-2.0-2 Cs2 Filter Add UEs into cs2Filter (ID: 13452316)

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13452317`)

Cs2 Filter At the end of DlTd scheduling(cs2List is ready), all UEs in cs2List shall be added into Cs2Filter before DL TD EO sends the cs2List with message FdScheduleReq/FdmScheduleReq(see [13448852: New Internal Messages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlFfYCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) to the DL FD EO.

---

##### 2.2.11.2.0-2.0-3 Cs2 Filter Remove UEs from cs2Filter (ID: 13452318)

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13452319`)

Cs2 Filter Upon FdmScheduleResp(see [13448852: New Internal Messages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlFfYCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) or FdScheduleResp is received, the UEs included in the messages shall be removed from Cs2Filter.

Rational:

- After DlFdm is done, the Ues which are not selected to be scheduled in current slot shall be scheduling eligble UEs as soon as posible in next slot.

- For Ues which is dropped by FD-UE skipping (see [11213118: FD-UE Skipping](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be send back up DL TD EO in FdScheduleResp to avoid zombie UEs in cs2Filter.

---

#### 2.2.11.2.0-3 Cs2 Filter Apply on UE message (ID: 13448766)
##### 2.2.11.2.0-3.0-1 Cs2 Filter Filter UE message (ID: 13452391)

**2.2.11.2.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448767`)

Cs2 Filter When the UE related messages are received and the UE(s) in the message is in cs2Filter, the messages can NOT be handled immediately to avoid data race.

The message(s) shall be buffered into BufferedEvents(a list stores the messages blocked by Cs2Filter), and recorded the related (UE, msg) information in FilteredEvents(includes [UE, message] pair blocked by Cs2Filter).

If there are more than one UEs in single message, the UEs are not in Cs2Filter can be handled immediately. The message still shall be buffered in case there are other UEs in cs2Filter in the message. The handled UEs in the message shall be skipped when the message is retrieved to handle.

Once the UE is removed from Cs2Filter, the buffered message shall be retrieved and handled as soon as possible.

The impacted messages refer to [Message.xlsx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB014500%20-%20CB014999/CFAM/CB014670%20Extended%20downlink%20processing%20configuration%20for%20FR1-TDD/Message.xlsx?d=w635cc1f1a29545469c0a8febba482e6a&csf=1&web=1&e=1IzQui) .

---

##### 2.2.11.2.0-3.0-2 Cs2 Filter Restriction (ID: 13452392)

**2.2.11.2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13452393`)

Cs2 Filter With Cs2Filter is applied on UE message handling, the following rules shall be obeyed.

- The messages priority shall not be changed.

- For a single UE, the message handling may be delayed, but the messages handling sequence of the UE shall not be changed.

- For a UE, when it is removed from Cs2Filter, NRT message handling shall not exceed time budget limitations of current slot (OLC applied).

---

#### 2.2.11.2.0-4 Cs2 Filter Cell Message Handling (ID: 13448762)

**2.2.11.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13448763`)

Cs2 Filter According to CellDb Split solution in Feature CB014822, Dl FD EO can visit CellDb directly. So, if DL TD EO is modifying CellDb when DL FD EO is reading, data race will be introduced.

To avoid conflict, when the cell level messages received,

If FdScheduleReq N (N is the xsfn) is send but the corresponding FdScheduleResp N is not received/handled, the cell messages shall be buffered and set cs1Size([11212970: Control based on run-time measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) as 1.

When FdScheduleResp N is received and handled, before FdScheduleReq N+1 sending, the buffered cell messages can be handled.

After all buffered cell message handled,

cs1Size shall restore as [11212970: Control based on run-time measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

The impacted messages refer to [Message.xlsx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB014500%20-%20CB014999/CFAM/CB014670%20Extended%20downlink%20processing%20configuration%20for%20FR1-TDD/Message.xlsx?d=w635cc1f1a29545469c0a8febba482e6a&csf=1&web=1&e=1IzQui) .

---

Cs2 Filter This requirement defines the bitset to record the messages filtered by cs2Filter or buffered cell messages in a specific period.

 buffer, pop, handle

### 2.2.11.3 DL Parallel Scheduler (ID: 13448847)
#### 2.2.11.3.0-1 DL Parallel Scheduler Advance Scheduling Timing (ID: 13448848)

**2.2.11.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448849`)

DL Parallel Scheduler rd parameter, default = 150us

---

#### 2.2.11.3.0-2 DL Parallel Scheduler Scheduling Sequence (ID: 13451424)

**2.2.11.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13451425`)

DL Parallel Scheduler pre/td/post/nrt can parallely run with fdm/fd in pipeline slot

post(n) may before or after pre(n+1) normal pipeline slot

post(n) shall before pre(n+1) in last pipeline slot

same as legacy in non-pipeline slot

---

#### 2.2.11.3.0-3 DL Parallel Scheduler TD EO Split(Optinal) (ID: 13448850)

**2.2.11.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13448851`)

DL Parallel Scheduler legacy requirement update:

Details decided by implementation

high level picture:

-FDM scheduler move from TD to FD

-Core selection for FD EO

-post timerwheel callback move to post TD

-DlToUlIntraSchedUpdate move to post TD for normal pipeline slot
